        // ============================================================
        // SECTION: EDIT XP â€” Search member
        // ============================================================
        window.searchMemberForXP = function(query) {
            const dropdown = document.getElementById('xpMemberDropdown');

            if (!query || query.length < 2) {
                dropdown.classList.add('hidden');
                return;
            }

            const results = allMembers.filter(m =>
                (m.name || '').toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase()) ||
                (m.memberId || '').toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase())
            ).slice(0, 8);

            if (results.length === 0) {
                dropdown.classList.add('hidden');
                return;
            }

            dropdown.innerHTML = results.map(m => `
                <div class="p-3 hover:bg-white/5 cursor-pointer flex items-center gap-3 border-b border-white/5 last:border-0"
                     onclick="selectXPMember('${m.id}')">
                    <div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-ng-red/20 border border-ng-red/30 flex items-center justify-center text-ng-red font-bold text-xs">
                        ${(m.name || 'U')[0]}
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <p class="text-white text-sm font-semibold">${escHtml(m.name)}</p>
                        <p class="text-gray-500 text-xs mono">${escHtml(m.memberId || m.id)}</p>
                    </div>
                    <div class="ml-auto text-right">
                        <p class="text-white font-bold font-display">${m.xpCache || 0}</p>
                        <p class="text-gray-500 text-xs">XP</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `).join('');

            dropdown.classList.remove('hidden');
        };

        window.selectXPMember = function(uid) {
            const member = allMembers.find(m => m.id === uid);
            if (!member) return;

            xpTargetUserId = uid;
            document.getElementById('xpMemberDropdown').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('xpMemberSearch').value = member.name;
            document.getElementById('xpSelectedMember').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('xpMemberAvatar').textContent = (member.name || 'U')[0];
            document.getElementById('xpMemberName').textContent = member.name || '-';
            document.getElementById('xpMemberId').textContent = member.memberId || uid;
            document.getElementById('xpCurrentValue').textContent = member.xpCache || 0;
            document.getElementById('xpNewValue').value = member.xpCache || 0;
        };

        window.updateXPDiff = function() {
            const diffEl = document.getElementById('xpDiffText');
            const member = allMembers.find(m => m.id === xpTargetUserId);
            if (!member) { diffEl.classList.add('hidden'); return; }

            const newVal = parseInt(document.getElementById('xpNewValue').value) || 0;
            const diff = newVal - (member.xpCache || 0);

            diffEl.classList.remove('hidden');
            if (diff > 0) {
                diffEl.textContent = `+${diff} XP will be added`;
                diffEl.className = 'text-xs mt-1 text-green-400';
            } else if (diff < 0) {
                diffEl.textContent = `${diff} XP will be deducted`;
                diffEl.className = 'text-xs mt-1 text-red-400';
            } else {
                diffEl.textContent = 'No change';
                diffEl.className = 'text-xs mt-1 text-gray-500';
            }
        };

        window.submitXPEdit = async function() {
            if (!xpTargetUserId) { showToast('Select a member first', 'error'); return; }

            const newXP = parseInt(document.getElementById('xpNewValue').value);
            const reason = document.getElementById('xpReason').value.trim();

            if (isNaN(newXP) || newXP < 0) { showToast('XP must be 0 or greater', 'error'); return; }
            if (reason.length < 5) { showToast('Reason must be at least 5 characters', 'error'); return; }

            const member = allMembers.find(m => m.id === xpTargetUserId);
            const oldXP = member?.xpCache || 0;

            const btn = document.getElementById('btnSubmitXP');
            btn.disabled = true;
            btn.textContent = 'Applying...';

            try {
                await updateDoc(doc(db, 'users', xpTargetUserId), { xpCache: newXP });

                await addDoc(collection(db, 'xpHistory'), {
                    userId: xpTargetUserId,
                    oldXP,
                    newXP,
                    change: newXP - oldXP,
                    reason,
                    changedBy: currentUser.uid,
                    changedByRole: currentRole,
                    type: 'manual',
                    timestamp: serverTimestamp()
                });

                await addDoc(collection(db, 'logs'), {
                    userId: currentUser.uid,
                    targetUserId: xpTargetUserId,
                    action: 'manual_xp_edit',
                    result: 'success',
                    oldXP,
                    newXP,
                    reason,
                    timestamp: serverTimestamp()
                });

                showToast(`XP updated: ${oldXP} â†’ ${newXP}`, 'success');
                document.getElementById('xpNewValue').value = '';
                document.getElementById('xpReason').value = '';
                xpTargetUserId = null;
                document.getElementById('xpSelectedMember').classList.add('hidden');
                document.getElementById('xpMemberSearch').value = '';

                // Refresh member list dan riwayat XP
                await loadMembers();
                await loadXPHistory();

            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Failed to update XP', 'error');
            } finally {
                btn.disabled = false;
                btn.textContent = 'Apply XP Change';
            }
        };

        async function loadXPHistory() {
            try {
                const q = query(collection(db, 'xpHistory'), where('type', '==', 'manual'), orderBy('timestamp', 'desc'), limit(20));
                const snap = await getDocs(q);

                if (snap.empty) {
                    document.getElementById('xpHistoryList').innerHTML =
                        '<p class="text-gray-500 text-sm">No manual XP edits yet.</p>';
                    return;
                }

                const html = snap.docs.map(d => {
                    const h = d.data();
                    const ts = h.timestamp ? h.timestamp.toDate().toLocaleString('en-US', {
                        month: 'short', day: 'numeric', hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit'
                    }) : '-';
                    const diff = h.newXP - h.oldXP;
                    return `
                        <div class="py-2 border-b border-white/5 last:border-0">
                            <div class="flex items-center justify-between mb-0.5">
                                <p class="text-white text-xs font-semibold mono">${escHtml(h.userId || '-')}</p>
                                <span class="text-xs font-bold ${diff >= 0 ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-red-400'}">
                                    ${diff >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${diff} XP
                                </span>
                            </div>
                            <p class="text-gray-500 text-xs">${escHtml(h.reason || '-')}</p>
                            <p class="text-gray-600 text-xs">${ts}</p>
                        </div>
                    `;
                }).join('');

                document.getElementById('xpHistoryList').innerHTML = html;

            } catch (err) {
                document.getElementById('xpHistoryList').innerHTML =
                    '<p class="text-gray-500 text-sm">Failed to load XP history.</p>';
            }
        }

        // ============================================================
        // SECTION: LEAVE REQUESTS
        // ============================================================
        async function loadLeaveRequests() {
            const filterStatus = document.getElementById('leaveFilter').value;
            try {
                let q;
                if (filterStatus) {
                    q = query(collection(db, 'leaveRequests'), where('status', '==', filterStatus), orderBy('createdAt', 'desc'), limit(50));
                } else {
                    q = query(collection(db, 'leaveRequests'), orderBy('createdAt', 'desc'), limit(50));
                }

                const snap = await getDocs(q);

                if (snap.empty) {
                    document.getElementById('leaveTableBody').innerHTML =
                        '<tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center text-gray-500 py-8">No leave requests found</td></tr>';
                    return;
                }

                const html = snap.docs.map(d => {
                    const req = d.data();
                    const ts = req.createdAt ? req.createdAt.toDate().toLocaleString('en-US', {
                        month: 'short', day: 'numeric', hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit'
                    }) : '-';
                    const statusColors = { pending: 'badge-afk', approved: 'badge-active', rejected: 'badge-resign', cancelled: 'badge-resign' };

                    return `
                        <tr>
                            <td class="mono text-xs text-gray-400">${escHtml(req.userId || '-')}</td>
                            <td class="text-gray-400 text-xs">${escHtml(req.eventId || '-')}</td>
                            <td class="text-gray-300 text-sm max-w-xs truncate">${escHtml(req.reason || '-')}</td>
                            <td class="text-gray-500 text-xs">${ts}</td>
                            <td><span class="badge ${statusColors[req.status] || 'badge-resign'}">${req.status}</span></td>
                            <td>
                                ${req.status === 'pending' ? `
                                    <div class="flex gap-1">
                                        <button onclick="processLeave('${d.id}', true)" class="btn-success text-xs py-1 px-2">Approve</button>
                                        <button onclick="processLeave('${d.id}', false)" class="btn-danger text-xs py-1 px-2">Reject</button>
                                    </div>
                                ` : '<span class="text-gray-600 text-xs">Processed</span>'}
                            </td>
                        </tr>
                    `;
                }).join('');

                document.getElementById('leaveTableBody').innerHTML = html;

            } catch (err) {
                console.error('loadLeaveRequests error:', err);
            }
        }

        window.processLeave = async function(requestId, approved) {
            try {
                const requestRef = doc(db, 'leaveRequests', requestId);
                const requestSnap = await getDoc(requestRef);
                if (!requestSnap.exists()) { showToast('Request not found', 'error'); return; }

                const request = requestSnap.data();

                await updateDoc(requestRef, {
                    status: approved ? 'approved' : 'rejected',
                    processedBy: currentUser.uid,
                    processedAt: serverTimestamp()
                });

                if (approved) {
                    const attendanceId = `${request.eventId}_${request.userId}`;
                    await setDoc(doc(db, 'attendance', attendanceId), {
                        eventId: request.eventId,
                        userId: request.userId,
                        status: 'excused',
                        xpChange: 0,
                        approvedBy: currentUser.uid,
                        attendedAt: serverTimestamp()
                    });
                }

                await addDoc(collection(db, 'notifications'), {
                    userId: request.userId,
                    type: 'leave_request',
                    message: approved ? 'Your leave request has been approved' : 'Your leave request has been rejected',
                    read: false,
                    createdAt: serverTimestamp()
                });

                await addDoc(collection(db, 'logs'), {
                    userId: currentUser.uid,
                    targetUserId: request.userId,
                    action: approved ? 'approve_leave' : 'reject_leave',
                    result: 'success',
                    timestamp: serverTimestamp()
                });

                showToast(`Leave request ${approved ? 'approved' : 'rejected'}`, 'success');
                await loadLeaveRequests();

            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Failed to process request', 'error');
            }
        };

        // ============================================================
        // SECTION: ANOMALIES
        // ============================================================
        async function loadAnomalies() {
            try {
                const q = query(collection(db, 'anomalies'), orderBy('timestamp', 'desc'), limit(50));
                const snap = await getDocs(q);

                if (snap.empty) {
                    document.getElementById('anomalyTableBody').innerHTML =
                        '<tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center text-gray-500 py-8">No anomalies detected</td></tr>';
                    return;
                }

                const html = snap.docs.map(d => {
                    const a = d.data();
                    const ts = a.timestamp ? a.timestamp.toDate().toLocaleString('en-US', {
                        month: 'short', day: 'numeric', hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit'
                    }) : '-';
                    const scoreColor = a.score >= 6 ? 'text-red-400' : a.score >= 3 ? 'text-yellow-400' : 'text-blue-400';

                    return `
                        <tr>
                            <td class="mono text-xs text-gray-400">${escHtml(a.userId || '-')}</td>
                            <td><span class="font-display font-bold text-xl ${scoreColor}">${a.score || 0}</span></td>
                            <td class="text-gray-400 text-xs">${(a.reasons || []).join(', ')}</td>
                            <td class="mono text-xs text-gray-600">${(a.deviceFingerprint || '-').slice(0, 16)}...</td>
                            <td class="text-gray-500 text-xs">${ts}</td>
                            <td>
                                <button onclick="suspendUser('${a.userId}')" class="btn-danger text-xs py-1 px-2">Suspend</button>
                            </td>
                        </tr>
                    `;
                }).join('');

                document.getElementById('anomalyTableBody').innerHTML = html;

            } catch (err) {
                console.error('loadAnomalies error:', err);
            }
        }

        window.suspendUser = async function(uid) {
            if (!uid || !confirm(`Suspend this user?`)) return;
            try {
                await updateDoc(doc(db, 'users', uid), {
                    status: 'suspended',
                    suspendedAt: serverTimestamp(),
                    suspendedBy: currentUser.uid
                });
                await addDoc(collection(db, 'logs'), {
                    userId: currentUser.uid,
                    targetUserId: uid,
                    action: 'suspend_user',
                    result: 'success',
                    timestamp: serverTimestamp()
                });
                showToast('User suspended', 'success');
                await loadAnomalies();
            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Failed to suspend user', 'error');
            }
        };

        // ============================================================
        // SECTION: LOGS
        // ============================================================
        async function loadLogs() {
            lastLogDoc = null;
            await fetchLogs(false);
        }

        async function fetchLogs(loadMore) {
            const filterAction = document.getElementById('logFilterAction').value;
            const filterResult = document.getElementById('logFilterResult').value;

            try {
                let constraints = [orderBy('timestamp', 'desc'), limit(30)];
                if (filterAction) constraints.unshift(where('action', '==', filterAction));
                if (filterResult) constraints.unshift(where('result', '==', filterResult));
                if (loadMore && lastLogDoc) constraints.push(startAfter(lastLogDoc));

                const q = query(collection(db, 'logs'), ...constraints);
                const snap = await getDocs(q);

                lastLogDoc = snap.docs[snap.docs.length - 1] || null;
                document.getElementById('btnLoadMoreLogs').classList.toggle('hidden', snap.size < 30);

                if (snap.empty && !loadMore) {
                    document.getElementById('logsTableBody').innerHTML =
                        '<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center text-gray-500 py-8">No logs found</td></tr>';
                    return;
                }

                const actionColors = {
                    attend: 'text-green-400',
                    close_event: 'text-blue-400',
                    manual_xp_edit: 'text-yellow-400',
                    import_members: 'text-purple-400',
                    update_role: 'text-orange-400',
                    approve_leave: 'text-green-400',
                    reject_leave: 'text-red-400',
                    suspend_user: 'text-red-400',
                    create_event: 'text-blue-400'
                };

                const html = snap.docs.map(d => {
                    const l = d.data();
                    const ts = l.timestamp ? l.timestamp.toDate().toLocaleString('en-US', {
                        month: 'short', day: 'numeric', hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', second: '2-digit'
                    }) : '-';
                    const details = l.reason || l.newRole || l.eventName || l.totalImported ? (
                        l.reason || (l.newRole ? `â†’ ${l.newRole}` : '') ||
                        (l.eventName ? l.eventName : '') ||
                        (l.totalImported ? `${l.totalImported} members` : '')
                    ) : '';

                    return `
                        <tr>
                            <td class="mono text-xs text-gray-600">${ts}</td>
                            <td class="mono text-xs text-gray-400">${escHtml((l.userId || '-').slice(0, 12))}...</td>
                            <td><span class="mono text-xs font-semibold ${actionColors[l.action] || 'text-gray-400'}">${escHtml(l.action || '-')}</span></td>
                            <td><span class="badge ${l.result === 'success' ? 'badge-active' : 'badge-suspended'}">${l.result || '-'}</span></td>
                            <td class="text-gray-500 text-xs max-w-xs truncate">${escHtml(details)}</td>
                        </tr>
                    `;
                }).join('');

                const tbody = document.getElementById('logsTableBody');
                if (loadMore) {
                    tbody.innerHTML += html;
                } else {
                    tbody.innerHTML = html;
                }

            } catch (err) {
                console.error('fetchLogs error:', err);
            }
        }

        window.loadMoreLogs = function() { fetchLogs(true); };

        window.exportLogsCSV = async function() {
            try {
                const q = query(collection(db, 'logs'), orderBy('timestamp', 'desc'), limit(500));
                const snap = await getDocs(q);
                const rows = [['Timestamp', 'User ID', 'Action', 'Result', 'Details']];
                snap.docs.forEach(d => {
                    const l = d.data();
                    rows.push([
                        l.timestamp ? l.timestamp.toDate().toISOString() : '-',
                        l.userId || '-',
                        l.action || '-',
                        l.result || '-',
                        l.reason || l.eventName || l.newRole || ''
                    ]);
                });
                downloadCSV(rows, 'system_logs_export.csv');
                showToast('Logs exported', 'success');
            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Failed to export logs', 'error');
            }
        };

        // ============================================================
        // Navigation â€” ganti section yang ditampilkan

        window.showSection = async function(name) {
            // Sembunyikan semua section
            document.querySelectorAll('[id^="section-"]').forEach(s => s.classList.add('hidden'));
            document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(n => n.classList.remove('active'));

            // Tampilkan section yang dipilih
            const section = document.getElementById(`section-${name}`);
            if (section) {
                section.classList.remove('hidden');
                section.classList.add('section-fade');
                setTimeout(() => section.classList.remove('section-fade'), 400);
            }

            const navItem = document.getElementById(`nav-${name}`);
            if (navItem) navItem.classList.add('active');

            // Load data saat section dibuka
            switch (name) {
                case 'overview': await loadOverviewData(); break;
                case 'events': await loadEvents(); break;
                case 'qr': await loadQRSection(); break;
                case 'members': await loadMembers(); break;
                case 'xp': await loadMembers(); await loadXPHistory(); break;
                case 'leave': await loadLeaveRequests(); break;
                case 'anomalies': await loadAnomalies(); break;
                case 'logs': await loadLogs(); break;
            }

            // Tutup sidebar di mobile
            document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.remove('open');
        };

            document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('hidden');

        window.closeModal = function(id) {
            document.getElementById(id).classList.add('hidden');

        window.toggleScheduleDate = function() {

            document.getElementById('scheduleDateWrapper').classList.toggle('hidden', mode === 'now');

        window.handleLogout = async function() {

            if (attendanceUnsubscribe) attendanceUnsubscribe();
            await signOut(auth);
            window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
        };

        // ============================================================
        // Auto logout setelah 30 menit tidak aktif
        // ============================================================
        function setupAutoLogout() {
            let timeout;
            const TIMEOUT_MS = 30 * 60 * 1000;

            function resetTimer() {
                clearTimeout(timeout);
                timeout = setTimeout(() => {
                    clearInterval(qrInterval);
                    signOut(auth).then(() => {
                        window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
                    });
                }, TIMEOUT_MS);
            }

            ['mousedown', 'keypress', 'scroll', 'touchstart', 'click'].forEach(ev => {
                document.addEventListener(ev, resetTimer, true);
            });

            resetTimer();
        }

        // ============================================================
        // Helper: Generate token kriptografis
        // ============================================================
        function generateSecureToken(length = 32) {
            const arr = new Uint8Array(length);
            crypto.getRandomValues(arr);
            return Array.from(arr).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('').slice(0, length);
        }

        // Helper: generate password sementara
        function generateTempPasswordLocal() {
            const u = 'ABCDEFGHJKLMNPQRSTUVWXYZ';
            const l = 'abcdefghjkmnpqrstuvwxyz';
            const n = '23456789';
            const s = '!@#$%';
            const r = str => str[Math.floor(Math.random() * str.length)];
            return r(u) + r(l) + r(l) + r(l) + r(n) + r(n) + r(s) + r(l);
        }

        // Helper: Escape HTML untuk mencegah XSS
        function escHtml(str) {
            if (!str) return '';
            return String(str).replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
        }

        // Helper: Download CSV
        function downloadCSV(rows, filename) {
            const content = rows.map(r => r.map(cell => `"${String(cell).replace(/"/g, '""')}"`).join(',')).join('\n');
            const blob = new Blob([content], { type: 'text/csv;charset=utf-8;' });
            const a = document.createElement('a');
            a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
            a.download = filename;
            a.click();
        }

        // ============================================================
        // Toast notification
        // ============================================================
        window.showToast = function(message, type = 'info') {
            const container = document.getElementById('toastContainer');
            const toast = document.createElement('div');
            toast.className = `toast toast-${type}`;

            const icons = {
                success: '<svg class="w-4 h-4 flex-shrink-0" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M5 13l4 4L19 7"/></svg>',
                error: '<svg class="w-4 h-4 flex-shrink-0" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M6 18L18 6M6 6l12 12"/></svg>',
                info: '<svg class="w-4 h-4 flex-shrink-0" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M13 16h-1v-4h-1m1-4h.01M21 12a9 9 0 11-18 0 9 9 0 0118 0z"/></svg>'
            };

            toast.innerHTML = `${icons[type] || icons.info}<span>${escHtml(message)}</span>`;
            container.appendChild(toast);
            setTimeout(() => { toast.style.opacity = '0'; toast.style.transform = 'translateY(8px)'; toast.style.transition = 'all 0.3s ease'; setTimeout(() => toast.remove(), 300); }, 4000);
        };

    </script>
</body>
</html>

window.handleChangePassword = async function() {
    // Guard clause â€” pastikan auth sudah siap
    if (!authReady || !currentUser) {
        showError('Session not ready. Please refresh the page.');
        return;
    }

    const newPassword = document.getElementById('newPassword').value;
    const confirmPassword = document.getElementById('confirmPassword').value;

    if (!newPassword || !confirmPassword) {
        showError('Please fill in all fields');
        return;
    }

    const checks = {
        minLength: newPassword.length >= 8,
        hasUppercase: /[A-Z]/.test(newPassword),
        hasNumber: /[0-9]/.test(newPassword),
        hasSpecial: /[!@#$%^&*]/.test(newPassword)
    };

    if (!Object.values(checks).every(Boolean)) {
        showError('Password does not meet all requirements');
        return;
    }

    if (newPassword !== confirmPassword) {
        showError('Passwords do not match');
        return;
    }

    const btn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.textContent = 'Updating...';

    try {
        await updatePassword(currentUser, newPassword);

        await updateDoc(doc(db, 'users', currentUser.uid), {
            mustChangePassword: false,
            passwordChangedAt: serverTimestamp()
        });

        showSuccess('Password updated! Redirecting...');
        
        // Redirect setelah 2 detik
        setTimeout(() => {
            window.location.href = '/public/pages/dashboard.html';
        }, 2000);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Change password error:', error);

        if (error.code === 'auth/requires-recent-login') {
            showError('Session expired. Please sign in again.');
            await signOut(auth);
            window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
            return; // stop, jangan jalankan kode di bawah
        }

        showError('Failed to update password. Please try again.');
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.textContent = 'Set Password';
    }
};
        // Password strength checker
        window.checkStrength = function(password) {
            const checks = [
                password.length >= 8,
                /[A-Z]/.test(password),
                /[0-9]/.test(password),
                /[!@#$%^&*]/.test(password)
            ];
            const passed = checks.filter(Boolean).length;
            const colors = ['bg-red-500', 'bg-orange-500', 'bg-yellow-500', 'bg-green-500'];
            const labels = ['Min 8 characters', 'Uppercase letter', 'Number', 'Special character'];

            ['b1','b2','b3','b4'].forEach((id, i) => {
                document.getElementById(id).className =
                    `strength-bar flex-1 ${i < passed ? colors[passed-1] : 'bg-white/10'}`;
            });

            ['c1','c2','c3','c4'].forEach((id, i) => {
                const el = document.getElementById(id);
                el.textContent = (checks[i] ? '+ ' : '- ') + labels[i];
                el.className = `text-xs ${checks[i] ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-gray-500'}`;
            });
        };

        window.togglePwd = function(id, btn) {
            const input = document.getElementById(id);
            input.type = input.type === 'password' ? 'text' : 'password';
            btn.textContent = input.type === 'password' ? 'Show' : 'Hide';
        };

        function showError(msg) {
            document.getElementById('errorText').textContent = msg;
            document.getElementById('errorMsg').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('successMsg').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        function showSuccess(msg) {
            document.getElementById('successText').textContent = msg;
            document.getElementById('successMsg').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('errorMsg').classList.add('hidden');
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<script type="module">
    import { initializeApp, getApps } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js';
    import {
        getAuth, onAuthStateChanged, signOut
    } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-auth.js';
    import {
        getFirestore, doc, getDoc, collection, query, where,
        orderBy, limit, getDocs, addDoc, serverTimestamp, onSnapshot
    } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-firestore.js';

    // ============================================================
    // Konfigurasi Firebase â€” ganti dengan nilai asli kamu
    // ============================================================
    const firebaseConfig = {
            apiKey: "AIzaSyD6AqPbmW4UM1d1o8caBWSIi61yQsxxsGk",
            authDomain: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebaseapp.com",
            projectId: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame",
            storageBucket: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebasestorage.app",
            messagingSenderId: "377822320778",
            appId: "1:377822320778:web:f7305bb71019f670ccf573"
    };

         // BARU â€” cek dulu sebelum inisialisasi
    import { initializeApp, getApps } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js';
    const app = getApps().length === 0 ? initializeApp(firebaseConfig) : getApps()[0];
    const auth = getAuth(app);
    const db = getFirestore(app);

    let currentUser = null;
    let userData = null;
    let xpHistoryData = [];

    // ============================================================
    // Cek auth â€” redirect jika belum login
    // ============================================================
    onAuthStateChanged(auth, async (user) => {
        if (!user || !user.emailVerified) {
            window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
            return;
        }
        currentUser = user;
        await loadDashboard();
        setupAutoLogout();
        loadNotifications();
    });

    // ============================================================
    // Load semua data dashboard
    // ============================================================
    async function loadDashboard() {
        try {
            // Ambil data user
            const userDoc = await getDoc(doc(db, 'users', currentUser.uid));
            if (!userDoc.exists()) {
                await signOut(auth);
                window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
                return;
            }

            userData = userDoc.data();

            // Redirect jika harus ganti password
            if (userData.mustChangePassword) {
                window.location.href = '/public/pages/change-password.html';
                return;
            }

            // Tampilkan konten
            document.getElementById('loadingState').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('dashContent').classList.remove('hidden');

            renderProfile();
            renderStats();
            setupAdminNav();
            await loadAttendanceHistory();
            await loadXPHistory();
            await loadLeaveRequests();
            await loadAchievements();
            checkActiveEvent();
            renderDate();

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Dashboard load error:', error);
        }
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Render profil user
    // ============================================================
    function renderProfile() {
        const initial = userData.name ? userData.name[0].toUpperCase() : '?';
        const xp = userData.xpCache || 0;
        const level = Math.floor(xp / 100) + 1;
        const progress = xp % 100;

        document.getElementById('avatarInitial').textContent = initial;
        document.getElementById('profileInitial').textContent = initial;
        document.getElementById('headerName').textContent = userData.name;
        document.getElementById('profileName').textContent = userData.name;
        document.getElementById('profileDivision').textContent = userData.division || '-';
        document.getElementById('profileTeam').textContent = userData.team ? `Team: ${userData.team}` : '';
        document.getElementById('profileLevel').textContent = level;
        document.getElementById('profileXP').textContent = xp;
        document.getElementById('profileNextXP').textContent = level * 100;
        document.getElementById('xpBarFill').style.width = `${progress}%`;
        document.getElementById('streakCount').textContent = userData.streak || 0;

        // Role badge
        const role = userData.role || 'member';
        const roleEls = [document.getElementById('headerRole'), document.getElementById('profileRoleBadge')];
        roleEls.forEach(el => {
            if (el) {
                el.textContent = role;
                el.className = `role-badge role-${role}`;
            }
        });

        // NPC badge
        if (role === 'npc') {
            document.getElementById('npcBadge').classList.remove('hidden');
        }

        // Stat XP
        document.getElementById('statXP').textContent = xp;
        document.getElementById('statAttended').textContent = userData.attendanceCount || 0;
        document.getElementById('statBestStreak').textContent = userData.bestStreak || userData.streak || 0;
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Render stats â€” attendance rate
    // ============================================================
    async function renderStats() {
        try {
            // Ambil total event yang sudah closed
            const eventsSnap = await getDocs(query(
                collection(db, 'events'),
                where('status', '==', 'closed')
            ));
            const totalEvents = eventsSnap.size;

            const attended = userData.attendanceCount || 0;
            const rate = totalEvents > 0 ? Math.round((attended / totalEvents) * 100) : 0;
            document.getElementById('statRate').textContent = `${rate}%`;

            // Hitung rank
            const allUsersSnap = await getDocs(query(
                collection(db, 'users'),
                where('status', '==', 'active'),
                orderBy('xpCache', 'desc')
            ));
            let rank = 1;
            allUsersSnap.forEach(d => {
                if ((d.data().xpCache || 0) > (userData.xpCache || 0)) rank++;
            });
            document.getElementById('statRank').textContent = rank;
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('Stats error:', e);
        }
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Load riwayat kehadiran
    // ============================================================
    async function loadAttendanceHistory() {
        try {
            const snap = await getDocs(query(
                collection(db, 'attendance'),
                where('userId', '==', currentUser.uid),
                orderBy('attendedAt', 'desc'),
                limit(10)
            ));

            const container = document.getElementById('attendanceList');

            if (snap.empty) {
                container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-500 text-sm text-center py-4">No attendance records yet</p>';
                return;
            }

            container.innerHTML = snap.docs.map(d => {
                const a = d.data();
                const status = a.status;
                const badgeClass = status === 'present' ? 'badge-present' : status === 'excused' ? 'badge-excused' : 'badge-absent';
                const xpText = a.xpChange > 0 ? `+${a.xpChange} XP` : a.xpChange < 0 ? `${a.xpChange} XP` : '0 XP';
                const xpColor = a.xpChange > 0 ? 'text-green-400' : a.xpChange < 0 ? 'text-red-400' : 'text-gray-400';
                const date = a.attendedAt ? formatDate(a.attendedAt.toDate()) : '-';
                return `
                <div class="flex items-center justify-between p-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-white/3 transition">
                    <div class="min-w-0 mr-2">
                        <p class="text-sm font-medium text-white truncate">${a.eventName || 'Event'}</p>
                        <p class="text-xs text-gray-500">${date}</p>
                    </div>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-2 flex-shrink-0">
                        <span class="text-xs ${xpColor} font-semibold">${xpText}</span>
                        <span class="text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-medium ${badgeClass}">${status}</span>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            }).join('');
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('Attendance load error:', e);
        }
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Load riwayat XP untuk chart
    // ============================================================
    async function loadXPHistory() {
        try {
            const snap = await getDocs(query(
                collection(db, 'xpHistory'),
                where('userId', '==', currentUser.uid),
                orderBy('timestamp', 'asc'),
                limit(100)
            ));

            xpHistoryData = snap.docs.map(d => d.data());
            renderXPChart(6);
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('XP history error:', e);
            renderXPChart(6); // render kosong
        }
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Render XP Chart
    // ============================================================
    let xpChart = null;
    window.updateChart = function() {
        const months = parseInt(document.getElementById('chartFilter').value);
        renderXPChart(months);
    };

    function renderXPChart(months) {
        const labels = [];
        const dataPoints = [];
        const now = new Date();

        for (let i = months - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
            const d = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth() - i, 1);
            labels.push(d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', year: '2-digit' }));

            const monthXP = xpHistoryData
                .filter(h => {
                    if (!h.timestamp) return false;
                    const hDate = h.timestamp.toDate ? h.timestamp.toDate() : new Date(h.timestamp);
                    return hDate.getFullYear() === d.getFullYear() && hDate.getMonth() === d.getMonth();
                })
                .reduce((sum, h) => sum + (h.change || 0), 0);
            dataPoints.push(Math.max(0, monthXP));
        }

        const ctx = document.getElementById('xpChart').getContext('2d');
        if (xpChart) xpChart.destroy();

        xpChart = new Chart(ctx, {
            type: 'bar',
            data: {
                labels,
                datasets: [{
                    label: 'XP Gained',
                    data: dataPoints,
                    backgroundColor: 'rgba(230,57,70,0.5)',
                    borderColor: '#E63946',
                    borderWidth: 1,
                    borderRadius: 4,
                }]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true,
                plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
                scales: {
                    x: { grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' }, ticks: { color: '#6b7280', font: { size: 11 } } },
                    y: { grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' }, ticks: { color: '#6b7280', font: { size: 11 } }, beginAtZero: true }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Load leave requests
    // ============================================================
    async function loadLeaveRequests() {
        try {
            const snap = await getDocs(query(
                collection(db, 'leaveRequests'),
                where('userId', '==', currentUser.uid),
                orderBy('createdAt', 'desc'),
                limit(5)
            ));

            const container = document.getElementById('leaveList');
            if (snap.empty) {
                container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-500 text-sm text-center py-4">No leave requests</p>';
                return;
            }

            container.innerHTML = snap.docs.map(d => {
                const r = d.data();
                const statusColors = {
                    pending: 'text-yellow-400 bg-yellow-400/10 border-yellow-400/30',
                    approved: 'text-green-400 bg-green-400/10 border-green-400/30',
                    rejected: 'text-red-400 bg-red-400/10 border-red-400/30',
                    cancelled: 'text-gray-400 bg-gray-400/10 border-gray-400/30'
                };
                const date = r.createdAt ? formatDate(r.createdAt.toDate()) : '-';
                return `
                <div class="flex items-center justify-between p-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-white/3 transition">
                    <div class="min-w-0 mr-2">
                        <p class="text-sm font-medium text-white truncate">${r.eventName || 'Event'}</p>
                        <p class="text-xs text-gray-500">${r.reason?.substring(0, 60) || '-'}</p>
                        <p class="text-xs text-gray-600">${date}</p>
                    </div>
                    <span class="text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border font-medium flex-shrink-0 ${statusColors[r.status] || statusColors.pending}">${r.status}</span>
                </div>`;
            }).join('');
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('Leave requests error:', e);
        }
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Load achievements
    // ============================================================
    async function loadAchievements() {
        // Achievement lokal berdasarkan data user â€” tidak butuh query tambahan
        const xp = userData.xpCache || 0;
        const attended = userData.attendanceCount || 0;
        const streak = userData.streak || 0;

        const achievements = [];

        if (attended >= 1) achievements.push({ icon: 'âœ“', label: 'First Attendance', desc: 'Attended your first event', color: 'bg-green-500/20' });
        if (attended >= 5) achievements.push({ icon: '5', label: 'Five Events', desc: 'Attended 5 events', color: 'bg-blue-500/20' });
        if (attended >= 10) achievements.push({ icon: '10', label: 'Ten Events', desc: 'Attended 10 events', color: 'bg-purple-500/20' });
        if (streak >= 3) achievements.push({ icon: 'S', label: 'On a Roll', desc: '3+ day attendance streak', color: 'bg-orange-500/20' });
        if (streak >= 7) achievements.push({ icon: 'S7', label: 'Week Warrior', desc: '7-day attendance streak', color: 'bg-red-500/20' });
        if (xp >= 100) achievements.push({ icon: 'XP', label: 'Century', desc: 'Reached 100 XP', color: 'bg-yellow-500/20' });
        if (xp >= 500) achievements.push({ icon: 'XP', label: 'Veteran', desc: 'Reached 500 XP', color: 'bg-yellow-500/20' });

        const container = document.getElementById('achievementList');
        if (achievements.length === 0) {
            container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-500 text-sm text-center py-4">No achievements yet â€” start attending events!</p>';
            return;
        }

        container.innerHTML = achievements.map(a => `
            <div class="achievement-card">
                <div class="achievement-icon ${a.color} text-white font-bold text-xs">${a.icon}</div>
                <div>
                    <p class="text-sm font-semibold text-white">${a.label}</p>
                    <p class="text-xs text-gray-500">${a.desc}</p>
                </div>
            </div>`).join('');
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Cek event aktif
    // ============================================================
    async function checkActiveEvent() {
        try {
            const snap = await getDocs(query(
                collection(db, 'events'),
                where('status', '==', 'active'),
                limit(1)
            ));

            if (!snap.empty) {
                const event = snap.docs[0].data();
                document.getElementById('activeEventCard').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('activeEventName').textContent = event.name;
                document.getElementById('activeEventXP').textContent = `+${event.xpReward || 10} XP for attendance`;
            }
        } catch (e) {}
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Load notifikasi
    // ============================================================
    async function loadNotifications() {
        try {
            const snap = await getDocs(query(
                collection(db, 'notifications'),
                where('userId', '==', currentUser.uid),
                where('read', '==', false),
                orderBy('createdAt', 'desc'),
                limit(10)
            ));

            if (!snap.empty) {
                document.getElementById('notifBadge').classList.remove('hidden');
                const container = document.getElementById('notifList');
                container.innerHTML = snap.docs.map(d => {
                    const n = d.data();
                    return `<div class="p-3 hover:bg-white/5 rounded-lg transition cursor-pointer" onclick="markRead('${d.id}', this)">
                        <p class="text-sm text-white">${n.message}</p>
                        <p class="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-0.5">${n.createdAt ? formatDate(n.createdAt.toDate()) : ''}</p>
                    </div>`;
                }).join('');
            }
        } catch (e) {}
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Setup admin nav â€” tampilkan hanya jika role yang sesuai
    // ============================================================
    function setupAdminNav() {
        const role = userData.role || 'member';
        if (['admin', 'inventori', 'superadmin', 'presiden'].includes(role)) {
            document.getElementById('adminNav').classList.remove('hidden');
        }
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Submit leave request
    // ============================================================
    window.openLeaveModal = async function() {
        // Load upcoming events
        try {
            const snap = await getDocs(query(
                collection(db, 'events'),
                where('status', 'in', ['scheduled', 'active'])
            ));
            const select = document.getElementById('leaveEventSelect');
            select.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Select event --</option>';
            snap.forEach(d => {
                const e = d.data();
                select.innerHTML += `<option value="${d.id}" data-name="${e.name}">${e.name}</option>`;
            });
        } catch (e) {}
        document.getElementById('leaveModal').classList.add('show');
    };

    window.closeLeaveModal = function() {
        document.getElementById('leaveModal').classList.remove('show');
    };

    window.submitLeaveRequest = async function() {
        const select = document.getElementById('leaveEventSelect');
        const reason = document.getElementById('leaveReason').value.trim();
        const eventId = select.value;
        const eventName = select.options[select.selectedIndex]?.dataset.name || '';

        if (!eventId) {
            document.getElementById('leaveError').textContent = 'Please select an event';
            document.getElementById('leaveError').classList.remove('hidden');
            return;
        }
        if (!reason || reason.length < 5) {
            document.getElementById('leaveError').textContent = 'Please provide a reason (min 5 characters)';
            document.getElementById('leaveError').classList.remove('hidden');
            return;
        }

        try {
            await addDoc(collection(db, 'leaveRequests'), {
                userId: currentUser.uid,
                userName: userData.name,
                eventId,
                eventName,
                reason,
                status: 'pending',
                createdAt: serverTimestamp()
            });

            closeLeaveModal();
            await loadLeaveRequests();
        } catch (e) {
            document.getElementById('leaveError').textContent = 'Failed to submit. Please try again.';
            document.getElementById('leaveError').classList.remove('hidden');
        }
    };

    // ============================================================
    // Helper: format tanggal
    // ============================================================
    function formatDate(date) {
        return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric' });
    }

    function renderDate() {
        document.getElementById('currentDate').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
            weekday: 'long', year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric'
        });
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Auto logout setelah 30 menit tidak aktif
    // ============================================================
    function setupAutoLogout() {
        let timer;
        const reset = () => {
            clearTimeout(timer);
            timer = setTimeout(async () => {
                await signOut(auth);
                window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
            }, 30 * 60 * 1000);
        };
        ['click','mousemove','keypress','scroll','touchstart'].forEach(e => document.addEventListener(e, reset));
        reset();
    }

    window.handleLogout = async function() {
        await signOut(auth);
        window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
    };

    window.toggleNotif = function() {
        document.getElementById('notifDropdown').classList.toggle('show');
    };

    window.markAllRead = function() {
        document.getElementById('notifDropdown').classList.remove('show');
        document.getElementById('notifBadge').classList.add('hidden');
    };

    window.toggleSidebar = function() {
        const sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar');
        const overlay = document.getElementById('mobileOverlay');
        sidebar.classList.toggle('open');
        overlay.classList.toggle('hidden');
    };

    // Tutup dropdown saat klik luar
    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        if (!e.target.closest('#notifDropdown') && !e.target.closest('button[onclick="toggleNotif()"]')) {
            document.getElementById('notifDropdown').classList.remove('show');
        }
    });
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script type="module">
    import { initializeApp, getApps } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js';
    import { getAuth, onAuthStateChanged, signOut } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-auth.js';
    import { getFirestore, collection, doc, getDoc, getDocs, query, where, orderBy } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-firestore.js';

    const firebaseConfig = {
            apiKey: "AIzaSyD6AqPbmW4UM1d1o8caBWSIi61yQsxxsGk",
            authDomain: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebaseapp.com",
            projectId: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame",
            storageBucket: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebasestorage.app",
            messagingSenderId: "377822320778",
            appId: "1:377822320778:web:f7305bb71019f670ccf573"
    };

         // BARU â€” cek dulu sebelum inisialisasi
    import { initializeApp, getApps } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js';
    const app = getApps().length === 0 ? initializeApp(firebaseConfig) : getApps()[0];
    const auth = getAuth(app);
    const db = getFirestore(app);

    let allRanked = [];
    let currentUid = null;

    onAuthStateChanged(auth, async (user) => {
        if (!user || !user.emailVerified) {
            window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
            return;
        }
        currentUid = user.uid;
        await loadLeaderboard();
        setupAutoLogout();
    });

    async function loadLeaderboard() {
        try {
            // Ambil semua user aktif, urutkan by XP
            const snap = await getDocs(query(
                collection(db, 'users'),
                where('status', 'in', ['active', 'npc']),
                orderBy('xpCache', 'desc')
            ));

            allRanked = snap.docs.map((d, i) => ({
                uid: d.id,
                rank: i + 1,
                ...d.data()
            }));

            // Populate division filter
            const divisions = [...new Set(allRanked.map(m => m.division).filter(Boolean))].sort();
            const divSelect = document.getElementById('filterDivision');
            divisions.forEach(div => {
                const opt = document.createElement('option');
                opt.value = div;
                opt.textContent = div;
                divSelect.appendChild(opt);
            });

            renderPodium();
            renderMyRank();
            applyFilter();

            document.getElementById('loadingState').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('mainContent').classList.remove('hidden');

        } catch (err) {
            console.error('Leaderboard error:', err);
        }
    }

    function renderPodium() {
        const top3 = allRanked.slice(0, 3);
        const podiumOrder = [top3[1], top3[0], top3[2]]; // 2nd, 1st, 3rd

        ['p2', 'p1', 'p3'].forEach((prefix, i) => {
            const m = podiumOrder[i];
            if (!m) {
                document.getElementById(`podium${i === 1 ? 1 : i === 0 ? 2 : 3}`).style.opacity = '0.3';
                return;
            }
            document.getElementById(`${prefix}avatar`).textContent = (m.name || 'U')[0].toUpperCase();
            document.getElementById(`${prefix}name`).textContent = m.name || '-';
            document.getElementById(`${prefix}div`).textContent = m.division || '-';
            document.getElementById(`${prefix}xp`).textContent = (m.xpCache || 0).toLocaleString();
        });
    }

    function renderMyRank() {
        const me = allRanked.find(m => m.uid === currentUid);
        if (!me) return;
        document.getElementById('myRankCard').classList.remove('hidden');
        document.getElementById('myRankNum').textContent = `#${me.rank}`;
        document.getElementById('myRankName').textContent = me.name || '-';
        document.getElementById('myRankXP').textContent = `${(me.xpCache || 0).toLocaleString()} XP`;
    }

    window.applyFilter = function() {
        const search = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase();
        const team = document.getElementById('filterTeam').value;
        const division = document.getElementById('filterDivision').value;
        const show = document.getElementById('filterShow').value;

        let filtered = allRanked.filter(m => {
            const matchSearch = !search || (m.name || '').toLowerCase().includes(search) || (m.memberId || '').toLowerCase().includes(search);
            const matchTeam = !team || m.team === team;
            const matchDiv = !division || m.division === division;
            return matchSearch && matchTeam && matchDiv;
        });

        // Re-rank dalam filter
        filtered = filtered.map((m, i) => ({ ...m, filteredRank: i + 1 }));

        if (show === 'top10') filtered = filtered.slice(0, 10);
        else if (show === 'top25') filtered = filtered.slice(0, 25);
        else if (show === 'top50') filtered = filtered.slice(0, 50);

        document.getElementById('rankCountLabel').textContent = `${filtered.length} member${filtered.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
        renderRankingTable(filtered);
    };

    function renderRankingTable(members) {
        if (members.length === 0) {
            document.getElementById('rankingBody').innerHTML =
                '<tr><td colspan="7" style="padding:40px;text-align:center;color:#6b7280;">No members match the filter</td></tr>';
            return;
        }

        document.getElementById('rankingBody').innerHTML = members.map((m, i) => {
            const rank = m.filteredRank || m.rank;
            const isMe = m.uid === currentUid;
            const level = Math.floor((m.xpCache || 0) / 100) + 1;

            let rankDisplay;
            if (rank === 1) rankDisplay = `<span class="rank-gold" style="font-size:20px;font-family:'Rajdhani',sans-serif;">#1</span>`;
            else if (rank === 2) rankDisplay = `<span class="rank-silver" style="font-size:18px;font-family:'Rajdhani',sans-serif;">#2</span>`;
            else if (rank === 3) rankDisplay = `<span class="rank-bronze" style="font-size:18px;font-family:'Rajdhani',sans-serif;">#3</span>`;
            else rankDisplay = `<span style="color:#6b7280;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;">#${rank}</span>`;

            const rowStyle = isMe
                ? 'background:rgba(230,57,70,0.07);border-left:3px solid #E63946;'
                : 'border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.04);';

            return `
                <tr style="${rowStyle}transition:background 0.15s;">
                    <td style="padding:12px 14px;">${rankDisplay}${isMe ? ' <span style="font-size:10px;color:#E63946;font-weight:700;">(you)</span>' : ''}</td>
                    <td style="padding:12px 14px;">
                        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;">
                            <div style="width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:50%;background:rgba(230,57,70,0.2);border:1px solid rgba(230,57,70,0.3);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;color:#E63946;font-weight:700;font-size:12px;flex-shrink:0;">
                                ${(m.name || 'U')[0].toUpperCase()}
                            </div>
                            <div>
                                <p style="color:white;font-weight:600;font-size:13px;">${esc(m.name || '-')}${m.role === 'npc' ? ' <span style="font-size:10px;background:rgba(139,92,246,0.2);color:#a78bfa;padding:1px 6px;border-radius:999px;border:1px solid rgba(139,92,246,0.3);">NPC</span>' : ''}</p>
                                <p style="color:#6b7280;font-size:11px;">${esc(m.memberId || '-')}</p>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </td>
                    <td style="padding:12px 14px;color:#9ca3af;font-size:12px;">${esc(m.division || '-')}</td>
                    <td style="padding:12px 14px;color:#9ca3af;font-size:12px;">${esc(m.team || '-')}</td>
                    <td style="padding:12px 14px;">
                        <span style="background:rgba(230,57,70,0.1);color:#E63946;border:1px solid rgba(230,57,70,0.3);padding:2px 8px;border-radius:999px;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;">Lv.${level}</span>
                    </td>
                    <td style="padding:12px 14px;text-align:right;color:white;font-weight:700;font-size:16px;font-family:'Rajdhani',sans-serif;">${(m.xpCache || 0).toLocaleString()}</td>
                    <td style="padding:12px 14px;color:#f59e0b;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;">&#128293; ${m.streak || 0}</td>
                </tr>`;
        }).join('');
    }

    function esc(s) { return String(s || '').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); }

    function setupAutoLogout() {
        let t;
        const r = () => { clearTimeout(t); t = setTimeout(async () => { await signOut(auth); window.location.href='/public/pages/login.html'; }, 30*60*1000); };
        ['click','keypress','scroll','touchstart'].forEach(e => document.addEventListener(e, r));
        r();
    }

    window.handleLogout = async () => { await signOut(auth); window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html'; };
</script>
</body>
</html>

            background: rgba(255,255,255,0.2);
            transition: all 0.3s ease;
        }
        .step-dot.active {
            background: #E63946;
            transform: scale(1.3);
        }
        .step-dot.done {
            background: #22c55e;
        }
    </style>
</head>

            <!-- pesan sukses global -->

                        class="w-full bg-white/5 text-white px-4 py-3 rounded-lg border border-white/10 transition placeholder-gray-600">
                </div>
                <div class="mb-6">
                    <label class="block text-gray-400 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">Password</label>
                    <div class="relative">
                        <input type="password" id="loginPassword" placeholder="â€¢â€¢â€¢â€¢â€¢â€¢â€¢â€¢"
                            class="w-full bg-white/5 text-white px-4 py-3 rounded-lg border border-white/10 transition placeholder-gray-600 pr-10">
                        <button type="button" onclick="togglePassword('loginPassword', this)"
                            class="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-300 text-xs">
                            Show
                        </button>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <button id="loginBtn" onclick="handleLogin()" class="btn-primary w-full text-white font-bold py-3 rounded-lg mb-3">
                    Sign In

                    <img src="https://www.google.com/favicon.ico" class="w-4 h-4">
                    Continue with Google

            <!-- ==================== FORM REGISTER ==================== -->
            <!-- Register dibagi 3 step:

            <div id="registerForm" class="hidden">

                <!-- step indicator -->
                <div class="flex items-center justify-center gap-2 mb-6">
                    <div class="step-dot active" id="dot1"></div>
                    <div class="h-px w-8 bg-white/20"></div>
                    <div class="step-dot" id="dot2"></div>
                    <div class="h-px w-8 bg-white/20"></div>
                    <div class="step-dot" id="dot3"></div>
                </div>

                <!-- step 1: verifikasi ID -->
                <div id="step1">
                    <h3 class="text-lg font-bold text-white mb-1">Verify Your Identity</h3>
                    <p class="text-gray-400 text-xs mb-4">Enter your member ID and temporary password provided by your admin</p>

                    <div class="mb-4">
                        <label class="block text-gray-400 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">Member ID</label>
                        <input type="text" id="memberId" placeholder="e.g. NG11018034PG"
                            class="w-full bg-white/5 text-white px-4 py-3 rounded-lg border border-white/10 transition placeholder-gray-600 uppercase"
                            oninput="this.value = this.value.toUpperCase()">
                    </div>
                    <div class="mb-6">

                                class="w-full bg-white/5 text-white px-4 py-3 rounded-lg border border-white/10 transition placeholder-gray-600 pr-10">
                            <button type="button" onclick="togglePassword('tempPassword', this)"

                                Show

                    <h3 class="text-lg font-bold text-white mb-1">Create Your Account</h3>
                    <p class="text-gray-400 text-xs mb-4">Set your email and a strong password</p>

                    <!-- info member yang terverifikasi -->
                    <div class="bg-green-500/10 border border-green-500/30 rounded-lg p-3 mb-4">
                        <p class="text-green-400 text-xs font-semibold">Identity Verified</p>
