                        <p class="text-gray-400 text-xs" id="verifiedDivision">-</p>
                    </div>

                    <div class="mb-4">
                        <label class="block text-gray-400 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">Email Address</label>
                        <input type="email" id="regEmail" placeholder="your@email.com"
                            class="w-full bg-white/5 text-white px-4 py-3 rounded-lg border border-white/10 transition placeholder-gray-600">
                    </div>

                    <div class="mb-2">
                        <label class="block text-gray-400 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">New Password</label>
                        <div class="relative">
                            <input type="password" id="newPassword" placeholder="Min 8 chars, uppercase, number, special"
                                class="w-full bg-white/5 text-white px-4 py-3 rounded-lg border border-white/10 transition placeholder-gray-600 pr-10"
                                oninput="checkPasswordStrength(this.value)">
                            <button type="button" onclick="togglePassword('newPassword', this)"
                                class="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-300 text-xs">
                                Show
                            </button>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <!-- password strength indicator -->
                    <div class="mb-4">
                        <div class="flex gap-1 mb-1">
                            <div class="strength-bar flex-1 bg-white/10" id="bar1"></div>
                            <div class="strength-bar flex-1 bg-white/10" id="bar2"></div>
                            <div class="strength-bar flex-1 bg-white/10" id="bar3"></div>
                            <div class="strength-bar flex-1 bg-white/10" id="bar4"></div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-1 mt-2">
                            <p class="text-xs" id="check-length">- Min 8 characters</p>
                            <p class="text-xs" id="check-upper">- Uppercase letter</p>
                            <p class="text-xs" id="check-number">- Number</p>
                            <p class="text-xs" id="check-special">- Special character (!@#$%^&*)</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <div class="mb-6">
                        <label class="block text-gray-400 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">Confirm Password</label>
                        <input type="password" id="confirmPassword" placeholder="Re-enter your password"
                            class="w-full bg-white/5 text-white px-4 py-3 rounded-lg border border-white/10 transition placeholder-gray-600">
                    </div>

                    <button onclick="handleRegister()" class="btn-primary w-full text-white font-bold py-3 rounded-lg">
                        Create Account
                    </button>
                </div>

                <!-- step 3: konfirmasi email -->
                <div id="step3" class="hidden text-center">
                    <div class="w-16 h-16 rounded-full bg-blue-500/20 border-2 border-blue-400 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
                        <svg class="w-8 h-8 text-blue-400" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                            <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M3 8l7.89 5.26a2 2 0 002.22 0L21 8M5 19h14a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2H5a2 2 0 00-2 2v10a2 2 0 002 2z"/>
                        </svg>
                    </div>
                    <h3 class="text-lg font-bold text-white mb-2">Check Your Email</h3>
                    <p class="text-gray-400 text-sm mb-2">We sent a verification link to:</p>
                    <p class="text-white font-semibold mb-4" id="sentEmailDisplay">-</p>
                    <p class="text-gray-500 text-xs mb-6">Click the link in the email, then come back here and click the button below</p>
                    <button onclick="checkEmailVerified()" class="btn-primary w-full text-white font-bold py-3 rounded-lg mb-3">
                        I Have Verified My Email
                    </button>
                    <button onclick="resendVerification()" class="w-full text-gray-400 hover:text-white text-sm py-2 transition">
                        Resend Email
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>

        </div>

        <!-- footer -->
        <p class="text-center text-gray-600 text-xs mt-6">2026 NEWGAME Organization. All rights reserved.</p>
    </div>

    <!-- Firebase SDK -->
    <script type="module">
        import { initializeApp, getApps } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js';
        import {
            getAuth,
            signInWithEmailAndPassword,
            createUserWithEmailAndPassword,
            sendEmailVerification,
            signInWithPopup,
            GoogleAuthProvider,
            onAuthStateChanged,
            signOut
        } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-auth.js';
        import {
            getFirestore,
            doc,
            setDoc,
            getDoc,
            serverTimestamp,
            initializeFirestore,
            CACHE_SIZE_UNLIMITED
        } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-firestore.js';

        // ============================================================
        // Konfigurasi Firebase â€” ganti dengan nilai asli kamu
        // ============================================================
        const firebaseConfig = {
            apiKey: "AIzaSyD6AqPbmW4UM1d1o8caBWSIi61yQsxxsGk",
            authDomain: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebaseapp.com",
            projectId: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame",
            storageBucket: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebasestorage.app",
            messagingSenderId: "377822320778",
            appId: "1:377822320778:web:f7305bb71019f670ccf573"
        };

             // BARU â€” cek dulu sebelum inisialisasi
        import { initializeApp, getApps } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js';
        const app = getApps().length === 0 ? initializeApp(firebaseConfig) : getApps()[0];
        const auth = getAuth(app);

        // Disable offline cache untuk halaman auth â€” mencegah data stale
        const db = initializeFirestore(app, {
            experimentalForceLongPolling: false
        });

        // State register â€” menyimpan data antar step
        let registerState = {
            memberId: null,
            memberData: null,
            email: null,
            userCredential: null
        };

        // ============================================================
        // Cek jika sudah login â€” redirect ke dashboard
        // ============================================================
        onAuthStateChanged(auth, async (user) => {
            if (user && user.emailVerified) {
                // Cek apakah sudah ganti password
                const userDoc = await getDoc(doc(db, 'users', user.uid));
                if (userDoc.exists() && userDoc.data().mustChangePassword) {
                    window.location.href = '/public/pages/change-password.html';
                } else if (userDoc.exists()) {
                    window.location.href = '/public/pages/dashboard.html';
                }
            }
        });

        // ============================================================
        // Switch tab login / register
        // ============================================================
        window.switchTab = function(tab) {
            const loginForm = document.getElementById('loginForm');
            const registerForm = document.getElementById('registerForm');
            const tabLogin = document.getElementById('tabLogin');
            const tabRegister = document.getElementById('tabRegister');

            if (tab === 'login') {
                loginForm.classList.remove('hidden');
                registerForm.classList.add('hidden');
                tabLogin.classList.add('active');
                tabRegister.classList.remove('active');
            } else {
                loginForm.classList.add('hidden');
                registerForm.classList.remove('hidden');
                tabLogin.classList.remove('active');
                tabRegister.classList.add('active');
            }
            hideMessages();
        };

        // ============================================================
        // Toggle show/hide password
        // ============================================================
        window.togglePassword = function(inputId, btn) {
            const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
            if (input.type === 'password') {
                input.type = 'text';
                btn.textContent = 'Hide';
            } else {
                input.type = 'password';
                btn.textContent = 'Show';
            }
        };

        // ============================================================
        // Password strength checker
        // ============================================================
        window.checkPasswordStrength = function(password) {
            const checks = {
                length: password.length >= 8,
                upper: /[A-Z]/.test(password),
                number: /[0-9]/.test(password),
                special: /[!@#$%^&*]/.test(password)
            };

            const passed = Object.values(checks).filter(Boolean).length;
            const colors = ['bg-red-500', 'bg-orange-500', 'bg-yellow-500', 'bg-green-500'];
            const bars = ['bar1', 'bar2', 'bar3', 'bar4'];

            bars.forEach((id, index) => {
                const bar = document.getElementById(id);
                bar.className = `strength-bar flex-1 ${index < passed ? colors[passed - 1] : 'bg-white/10'}`;
            });

            // Update checklist
            const checkEls = {
                'check-length': checks.length,
                'check-upper': checks.upper,
                'check-number': checks.number,
                'check-special': checks.special
            };

            const labels = {
                'check-length': 'Min 8 characters',
                'check-upper': 'Uppercase letter',
                'check-number': 'Number',
                'check-special': 'Special character (!@#$%^&*)'
            };

            Object.entries(checkEls).forEach(([id, ok]) => {
                const el = document.getElementById(id);
                el.textContent = (ok ? '+ ' : '- ') + labels[id];
                el.className = `text-xs ${ok ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-gray-500'}`;
            });
        };

        // ============================================================
        // STEP 1 â€” Verifikasi ID anggota + password sementara
        // ============================================================
        window.verifyMemberId = async function() {
            const memberId = document.getElementById('memberId').value.trim().toUpperCase();
            const tempPassword = document.getElementById('tempPassword').value;

            if (!memberId || !tempPassword) {
                showError('Please fill in all fields');
                return;
            }

            // Validasi format ID
            if (!memberId.startsWith('NG')) {
                showError('Invalid Member ID format. Must start with NG');
                return;
            }

            try {
                setLoading('verifyMemberId', true);

                // Cek ID di collection members
                const memberDoc = await getDoc(doc(db, 'members', memberId));

                if (!memberDoc.exists()) {
                    showError('Member ID not found. Contact your admin.');
                    return;
                }

                const memberData = memberDoc.data();

                // Cek status anggota
                if (!['ACTIVE', 'NPC'].includes(memberData.status)) {
                    showError('Your account is not active. Contact your admin.');
                    return;
                }

                // Cek sudah pernah register
                if (memberData.isRegistered) {
                    showError('This Member ID is already registered. Try signing in.');
                    return;
                }

                // Verifikasi password sementara
                if (tempPassword !== memberData.tempPassword) {
                    showError('Incorrect temporary password. Contact your admin.');
                    return;
                }

                // Simpan state untuk step berikutnya
                registerState.memberId = memberId;
                registerState.memberData = memberData;

                // Tampilkan info member
                document.getElementById('verifiedName').textContent = memberData.name;
                document.getElementById('verifiedDivision').textContent =
                    `${memberData.division} - ${memberData.team || 'No Team'}`;

                // Update step indicator
                updateStepIndicator(2);

                // Pindah ke step 2
                document.getElementById('step1').classList.add('hidden');
                document.getElementById('step2').classList.remove('hidden');

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Verify error:', error);
                showError('Verification failed. Please try again.');
            } finally {
                setLoading('verifyMemberId', false);
            }
        };

        // ============================================================
        // STEP 2 â€” Buat akun dengan email dan password baru
        // ============================================================
        window.handleRegister = async function() {
            const email = document.getElementById('regEmail').value.trim();
            const newPassword = document.getElementById('newPassword').value;
            const confirmPassword = document.getElementById('confirmPassword').value;

            if (!email || !newPassword || !confirmPassword) {
                showError('Please fill in all fields');
                return;
            }

            // Validasi password tidak sama dengan password sementara
            if (newPassword === registerState.memberData.tempPassword) {
                showError('New password cannot be the same as your temporary password');
                return;
            }

            // Validasi password baru
            const passwordChecks = {
                minLength: newPassword.length >= 8,
                hasUppercase: /[A-Z]/.test(newPassword),
                hasNumber: /[0-9]/.test(newPassword),
                hasSpecial: /[!@#$%^&*]/.test(newPassword)
            };

            if (!Object.values(passwordChecks).every(Boolean)) {
                showError('Password does not meet requirements');
                return;
            }

            if (newPassword !== confirmPassword) {
                showError('Passwords do not match');
                return;
            }

            try {
                setLoading('handleRegister', true);

                // Buat akun Firebase Auth
                const userCredential = await createUserWithEmailAndPassword(auth, email, newPassword);
                const user = userCredential.user;

                // Kirim email verifikasi
                await sendEmailVerification(user);

                // Simpan data user ke Firestore
                await setDoc(doc(db, 'users', user.uid), {
                    uid: user.uid,
                    memberId: registerState.memberId,
                    name: registerState.memberData.name,
                    email: email,
                    division: registerState.memberData.division,
                    team: registerState.memberData.team || '',
                    role: registerState.memberData.status === 'NPC' ? 'npc' : 'member',
                    status: 'active',
                    xpCache: 0,
                    attendanceCount: 0,
                    streak: 0,
                    mustChangePassword: false,
                    createdAt: serverTimestamp(),
                    lastLogin: serverTimestamp(),
                    sessionToken: crypto.randomUUID()
                });

                // Tandai member sudah register
                await setDoc(doc(db, 'members', registerState.memberId), {
                    isRegistered: true,
                    registeredUid: user.uid,
                    registeredAt: serverTimestamp()
                }, { merge: true });

                // Logout dulu â€” user harus verifikasi email
                registerState.email = email;
                registerState.userCredential = userCredential;
                await signOut(auth);

                // Update step indicator
                document.getElementById('sentEmailDisplay').textContent = email;
                updateStepIndicator(3);

                // Pindah ke step 3
                document.getElementById('step2').classList.add('hidden');
                document.getElementById('step3').classList.remove('hidden');

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Register error:', error);
                if (error.code === 'auth/email-already-in-use') {
                    showError('Email already registered. Try signing in.');
                } else if (error.code === 'auth/invalid-email') {
                    showError('Invalid email format');
                } else {
                    showError('Registration failed. Please try again.');
                }
            } finally {
                setLoading('handleRegister', false);
            }
        };

        // ============================================================
        // STEP 3 â€” Cek apakah email sudah diverifikasi
        // ============================================================
        window.checkEmailVerified = async function() {
            try {
                // Login sementara untuk cek status verifikasi
                const userCredential = await signInWithEmailAndPassword(
                    auth,
                    registerState.email,
                    document.getElementById('newPassword')?.value || ''
                );

                await userCredential.user.reload();

                if (userCredential.user.emailVerified) {
                    showSuccess('Email verified! Redirecting...');
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        window.location.href = '/public/pages/dashboard.html';
                    }, 1500);
                } else {
                    await signOut(auth);
                    showError('Email not verified yet. Please check your inbox.');
                }
            } catch (error) {
                showError('Verification check failed. Please try signing in manually.');
            }
        };

        // ============================================================
        // Kirim ulang email verifikasi
        // ============================================================
        window.resendVerification = async function() {
            try {
                const userCredential = await signInWithEmailAndPassword(
                    auth,
                    registerState.email,
                    document.getElementById('newPassword')?.value || ''
                );
                await sendEmailVerification(userCredential.user);
                await signOut(auth);
                showSuccess('Verification email resent. Check your inbox.');
            } catch (error) {
                showError('Failed to resend email. Please try again.');
            }
        };

        // ============================================================
        // LOGIN dengan email & password
        // ============================================================
        window.handleLogin = async function() {
            const email = document.getElementById('loginEmail').value.trim();
            const password = document.getElementById('loginPassword').value;

            if (!email || !password) {
                showError('Please fill in all fields');
                return;
            }

            try {
                const btn = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
                btn.disabled = true;
                btn.textContent = 'Signing in...';

                const userCredential = await signInWithEmailAndPassword(auth, email, password);
                const user = userCredential.user;

                // Cek email sudah diverifikasi
                if (!user.emailVerified) {
                    await signOut(auth);
                    showError('Email not verified. Check your inbox.');
                    return;
                }

                // Ambil data user
                const userDoc = await getDoc(doc(db, 'users', user.uid));
                if (!userDoc.exists()) {
                    await signOut(auth);
                    showError('Account data not found. Contact your admin.');
                    return;
                }

                const userData = userDoc.data();

                // Cek status akun
                if (userData.status === 'suspended') {
                    await signOut(auth);
                    showError('Your account has been suspended. Contact your admin.');
                    return;
                }

                // Update session
                await setDoc(doc(db, 'users', user.uid), {
                    lastLogin: serverTimestamp(),
                    sessionToken: crypto.randomUUID()
                }, { merge: true });

                // Redirect
                window.location.href = '/public/pages/dashboard.html';

            } catch (error) {
                if (error.code === 'auth/invalid-credential') {
                    showError('Incorrect email or password');
                } else if (error.code === 'auth/too-many-requests') {
                    showError('Too many attempts. Please try again later.');
                } else {
                    showError('Sign in failed. Please try again.');
                }
            } finally {
                const btn = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
                if (btn) {
                    btn.disabled = false;
                    btn.textContent = 'Sign In';
                }
            }
        };

        // ============================================================
        // LOGIN dengan Google
        // Google login hanya untuk yang sudah punya akun
        // ============================================================
        window.handleGoogleLogin = async function() {
            try {
                const provider = new GoogleAuthProvider();
                const userCredential = await signInWithPopup(auth, provider);
                const user = userCredential.user;

                // Cek apakah sudah punya akun di Firestore
                const userDoc = await getDoc(doc(db, 'users', user.uid));

                if (!userDoc.exists()) {
                    // Akun belum ada â€” user harus register dulu via ID
                    await signOut(auth);
                    showError('No account found. Please register with your Member ID first.');
                    return;
                }

                const userData = userDoc.data();

                if (userData.status === 'suspended') {
                    await signOut(auth);
                    showError('Your account has been suspended.');
                    return;
                }

                await setDoc(doc(db, 'users', user.uid), {
                    lastLogin: serverTimestamp(),
                    sessionToken: crypto.randomUUID()
                }, { merge: true });

                window.location.href = '/public/pages/dashboard.html';

            } catch (error) {
                if (error.code === 'auth/popup-closed-by-user') {
                    showError('Sign in cancelled');
                } else {
                    showError('Google sign in failed. Please try again.');
                }
            }
        };

        // ============================================================
        // Helper functions
        // ============================================================

        // Tampilkan error
        function showError(msg) {
            document.getElementById('errorText').textContent = msg;
            document.getElementById('errorMsg').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('successMsg').classList.add('hidden');
            setTimeout(() => {
                document.getElementById('errorMsg').classList.add('hidden');
            }, 5000);
        }

        // Tampilkan sukses
        function showSuccess(msg) {
            document.getElementById('successText').textContent = msg;
            document.getElementById('successMsg').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('errorMsg').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        // Sembunyikan semua pesan
        function hideMessages() {
            document.getElementById('errorMsg').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('successMsg').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        // Update step indicator
        function updateStepIndicator(currentStep) {
            for (let i = 1; i <= 3; i++) {
                const dot = document.getElementById(`dot${i}`);
                dot.className = 'step-dot';
                if (i < currentStep) dot.classList.add('done');
                else if (i === currentStep) dot.classList.add('active');
            }
        }

        // Loading state â€” disable semua tombol
        function setLoading(funcName, loading) {
            const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('button');
            buttons.forEach(btn => {
                if (loading) {
                    btn.disabled = true;
                    if (btn.dataset.loadingFor === funcName) {
                        btn.textContent = 'Please wait...';
                    }
                } else {
                    btn.disabled = false;
                }
            });
        }

        // Enter key untuk submit form login
        document.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                const loginForm = document.getElementById('loginForm');
                if (!loginForm.classList.contains('hidden')) {
                    handleLogin();
                }
            }
        });
    </script>

</body>
</html>

<script type="module">
    import { initializeApp, getApps } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js';
    import { getAuth, onAuthStateChanged, signOut } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-auth.js';
    import {
        getFirestore, collection, doc, getDoc, getDocs,
        query, where, orderBy, limit, startAfter
    } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-firestore.js';

    const firebaseConfig = {
            apiKey: "AIzaSyD6AqPbmW4UM1d1o8caBWSIi61yQsxxsGk",
            authDomain: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebaseapp.com",
            projectId: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame",
            storageBucket: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebasestorage.app",
            messagingSenderId: "377822320778",
            appId: "1:377822320778:web:f7305bb71019f670ccf573"
    };

         // BARU â€” cek dulu sebelum inisialisasi
    import { initializeApp, getApps } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js';
    const app = getApps().length === 0 ? initializeApp(firebaseConfig) : getApps()[0];
    const auth = getAuth(app);
    const db = getFirestore(app);

    let lastDoc = null;
    let allLogsCache = [];
    const PAGE = 50;

    onAuthStateChanged(auth, async (user) => {
        if (!user || !user.emailVerified) { window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html'; return; }
        const userDoc = await getDoc(doc(db, 'users', user.uid));
        if (!userDoc.exists()) { await signOut(auth); return; }
        const data = userDoc.data();
        if (!['admin','superadmin','presiden'].includes(data.role)) {
            window.location.href = '/public/pages/dashboard.html';
            return;
        }
        await loadStats();
        await loadLogs(true);
        setupAutoLogout();
    });

    async function loadStats() {
        try {
            const snap = await getDocs(collection(db, 'logs'));
            const logs = snap.docs.map(d => d.data());
            const today = new Date();
            today.setHours(0,0,0,0);

            document.getElementById('statTotal').textContent = logs.length;
            document.getElementById('statSuccess').textContent = logs.filter(l => l.result === 'success').length;
            document.getElementById('statFailed').textContent = logs.filter(l => l.result === 'failed').length;
            document.getElementById('statToday').textContent = logs.filter(l => {
                if (!l.timestamp) return false;
                const d = l.timestamp.toDate ? l.timestamp.toDate() : new Date(l.timestamp.seconds * 1000);
                return d >= today;
            }).length;
        } catch (e) { console.error(e); }
    }

    window.loadLogs = async function(reset = false) {
        if (reset) { lastDoc = null; document.getElementById('logsBody').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" style="padding:40px;text-align:center;color:#6b7280;">Loading...</td></tr>'; }

        const filterAction = document.getElementById('filterAction').value;
        const filterResult = document.getElementById('filterResult').value;
        const filterDate = document.getElementById('filterDate').value;
        const filterUser = document.getElementById('filterUser').value.trim();

        try {
            let constraints = [orderBy('timestamp', 'desc'), limit(PAGE)];
            if (filterAction) constraints.unshift(where('action', '==', filterAction));
            if (filterResult) constraints.unshift(where('result', '==', filterResult));
            if (lastDoc && !reset) constraints.push(startAfter(lastDoc));

            const q = query(collection(db, 'logs'), ...constraints);
            const snap = await getDocs(q);

            let logs = snap.docs.map(d => ({ id: d.id, ...d.data() }));

            // Filter tanggal dan user di client (Firestore range query terbatas)
            if (filterDate) {
                const day = new Date(filterDate);
                day.setHours(0,0,0,0);
                const dayEnd = new Date(filterDate);
                dayEnd.setHours(23,59,59,999);
                logs = logs.filter(l => {
                    if (!l.timestamp) return false;
                    const d = l.timestamp.toDate ? l.timestamp.toDate() : new Date(l.timestamp.seconds * 1000);
                    return d >= day && d <= dayEnd;
                });
            }
            if (filterUser) {
                logs = logs.filter(l => (l.userId || '').toLowerCase().includes(filterUser.toLowerCase()));
            }

            lastDoc = snap.docs[snap.docs.length - 1] || null;
            document.getElementById('btnLoadMore').classList.toggle('hidden', snap.size < PAGE);
            document.getElementById('logsCountLabel').textContent = `Showing ${reset ? logs.length : '...'} logs`;

            const actionColors = {
                attend: '#4ade80', close_event: '#60a5fa', create_event: '#60a5fa',
                manual_xp_edit: '#facc15', import_members: '#a78bfa',
                update_role: '#fb923c', update_member: '#fb923c',
                approve_leave: '#4ade80', reject_leave: '#f87171',
                suspend_user: '#f87171', set_initial_role: '#34d399'
            };

            const rows = logs.map(l => {
                const ts = l.timestamp ? (l.timestamp.toDate ? l.timestamp.toDate() : new Date(l.timestamp.seconds * 1000)).toLocaleString('en-US', {
                    month: 'short', day: 'numeric', hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', second: '2-digit'
                }) : '-';

                const details = [
                    l.reason, l.eventName, l.newRole ? `â†’ ${l.newRole}` : '',
                    l.totalImported ? `${l.totalImported} members` : '',
                    l.newXP !== undefined ? `XP: ${l.oldXP} â†’ ${l.newXP}` : '',
                    l.targetUserId ? `target: ${l.targetUserId.slice(0,8)}...` : ''
                ].filter(Boolean).join(' | ');

                const actionColor = actionColors[l.action] || '#9ca3af';

                return `
                    <tr style="border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.04);transition:background 0.15s;" onmouseover="this.style.background='rgba(255,255,255,0.02)'" onmouseout="this.style.background=''">
                        <td style="padding:10px 14px;font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;font-size:11px;color:#4b5563;">${ts}</td>
                        <td style="padding:10px 14px;font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;font-size:11px;color:#6b7280;">${esc((l.userId || '-').slice(0,16))}${l.userId && l.userId.length > 16 ? '...' : ''}</td>
                        <td style="padding:10px 14px;"><span style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;font-size:12px;font-weight:600;color:${actionColor};">${esc(l.action || '-')}</span></td>
                        <td style="padding:10px 14px;"><span class="badge badge-${l.result === 'success' ? 'success' : 'failed'}">${l.result || '-'}</span></td>
                        <td style="padding:10px 14px;font-size:12px;color:#6b7280;max-width:300px;" title="${esc(details)}">${esc(details.slice(0, 80))}${details.length > 80 ? '...' : ''}</td>
                    </tr>`;
            }).join('');

            if (reset) {
                document.getElementById('logsBody').innerHTML = rows || '<tr><td colspan="5" style="padding:40px;text-align:center;color:#6b7280;">No logs found</td></tr>';
            } else {
                document.getElementById('logsBody').innerHTML += rows;
            }

        } catch (err) {
            console.error('loadLogs error:', err);
            document.getElementById('logsBody').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" style="padding:40px;text-align:center;color:#f87171;">Failed to load logs</td></tr>';
        }
    };

    window.loadMore = () => loadLogs(false);

    window.clearFilters = function() {
        document.getElementById('filterAction').value = '';
        document.getElementById('filterResult').value = '';
        document.getElementById('filterDate').value = '';
        document.getElementById('filterUser').value = '';
        loadLogs(true);
    };

    window.exportLogs = async function() {
        try {
            const snap = await getDocs(query(collection(db, 'logs'), orderBy('timestamp', 'desc'), limit(1000)));
            const rows = [['Timestamp', 'User ID', 'Action', 'Result', 'Target User', 'Event', 'Reason', 'Old XP', 'New XP']];
            snap.docs.forEach(d => {
                const l = d.data();
                const ts = l.timestamp ? (l.timestamp.toDate ? l.timestamp.toDate() : new Date(l.timestamp.seconds * 1000)).toISOString() : '';
                rows.push([ts, l.userId || '', l.action || '', l.result || '', l.targetUserId || '', l.eventName || '', l.reason || '', l.oldXP ?? '', l.newXP ?? '']);
            });
            const csv = rows.map(r => r.map(c => `"${String(c).replace(/"/g,'""')}"`).join(',')).join('\n');
            const a = document.createElement('a');
            a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([csv], { type: 'text/csv' }));
            a.download = `system_logs_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.csv`;
            a.click();
        } catch (e) { alert('Export failed'); }
    };

    function esc(s) { return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); }

    function setupAutoLogout() {
        let t;
        const r = () => { clearTimeout(t); t = setTimeout(async () => { await signOut(auth); window.location.href='/public/pages/login.html'; }, 30*60*1000); };
        ['click','keypress','scroll','touchstart'].forEach(e => document.addEventListener(e, r));
        r();
    }

    window.handleLogout = async () => { await signOut(auth); window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html'; };
</script>
</body>
</html>

    // State
    let currentUserData = null;
    let allMembers = [...MEMBER_DATA];
    let filteredMembers = [...MEMBER_DATA];
    let firestoreXPMap = {};
    let currentPage = 1;
    const PAGE_SIZE = 20;

    // ============================================================
    // Auth check â€” ini yang fix masalah role hilang
    // ============================================================
    onAuthStateChanged(auth, async (user) => {
        if (!user || !user.emailVerified) {
            window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
            return;
        }

        try {
            const userDoc = await getDoc(doc(db, 'users', user.uid));
            if (!userDoc.exists()) {
                await signOut(auth);
                window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
                return;
            }

            currentUserData = userDoc.data();
            const role = currentUserData.role || 'member';
            const name = currentUserData.name || user.email;

            // Update sidebar info
            document.getElementById('sidebarName').textContent = name;
            document.getElementById('sidebarAvatar').textContent = name[0].toUpperCase();
            const roleBadge = document.getElementById('sidebarRoleBadge');
            roleBadge.textContent = role;
            roleBadge.className = `badge role-${role}`;

            // Tampilkan menu admin jika role yang sesuai
            if (['admin', 'inventori', 'superadmin', 'presiden'].includes(role)) {
                document.getElementById('adminNavSection').classList.remove('hidden');
            }

            // Sembunyikan loading overlay
            document.getElementById('loadingOverlay').classList.add('hidden');

            // Load XP dari Firestore untuk ditampilkan di tabel
            await loadFirestoreXP();

            // Render tabel
            updateStats();
            filterTable();

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Auth check error:', error);
            window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
        }
    });

    // ============================================================
    // Load XP semua user dari Firestore
    // Digabungkan dengan data CSV lokal
    // ============================================================
    async function loadFirestoreXP() {
        try {
            const snap = await getDocs(collection(db, 'users'));
            snap.forEach(d => {
                const data = d.data();
                if (data.memberId) {
                    firestoreXPMap[data.memberId] = {
                        xp: data.xpCache || 0,
                        role: data.role || 'member',
                        registered: true
                    };
                }
            });
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('loadFirestoreXP error:', e);
        }
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Stats
    // ============================================================
    function updateStats() {
        document.getElementById('statTotal').textContent = allMembers.length;
        document.getElementById('statActive').textContent = allMembers.filter(m => m.status === 'ACTIVE').length;
        document.getElementById('statAFK').textContent = allMembers.filter(m => m.status === 'AFK').length;
        document.getElementById('statNPC').textContent = allMembers.filter(m => m.status === 'NPC').length;
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Filter tabel
    // ============================================================
    window.filterTable = function() {
        const search = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase();
        const pillar = document.getElementById('filterPillar').value;
        const status = document.getElementById('filterStatus').value;
        const team   = document.getElementById('filterTeam').value;
        const gen    = document.getElementById('filterGen').value;

        filteredMembers = allMembers.filter(m => {
            const matchSearch = !search ||
                m.name.toLowerCase().includes(search) ||
                m.id.toLowerCase().includes(search);
            const matchPillar = !pillar || m.pillar === pillar;
            const matchStatus = !status || m.status === status;
            const matchTeam   = !team   || m.team === team;
            const matchGen    = !gen    || m.gen === gen;
            return matchSearch && matchPillar && matchStatus && matchTeam && matchGen;
        });

        currentPage = 1;
        renderTable();
    };

    // ============================================================
    // Render tabel dengan data gabungan CSV + Firestore
    // ============================================================
    function renderTable() {
        const start = (currentPage - 1) * PAGE_SIZE;
        const end   = start + PAGE_SIZE;
        const page  = filteredMembers.slice(start, end);
        const total = filteredMembers.length;

        document.getElementById('tableCountLabel').textContent = `${total} player${total !== 1 ? 's' : ''} found`;
        document.getElementById('paginationInfo').textContent  = `${Math.min(start+1,total)}â€“${Math.min(end,total)} of ${total}`;
        document.getElementById('btnPrev').disabled = currentPage === 1;
        document.getElementById('btnNext').disabled = end >= total;

        if (page.length === 0) {
            document.getElementById('tableBody').innerHTML =
                '<tr><td colspan="9" class="text-center text-gray-500 py-10">No players found</td></tr>';
            return;
        }

        const html = page.map(m => {
            const fsData = firestoreXPMap[m.id] || {};
            const xp = fsData.xp !== undefined ? fsData.xp : '-';
            const isRegistered = fsData.registered || false;
            const pillarClass = m.pillar === 'Game Logic' ? 'pillar-gl' : m.pillar === 'Game Design' ? 'pillar-gd' : 'pillar-gs';
            const pillarShort = m.pillar === 'Game Logic' ? 'GL' : m.pillar === 'Game Design' ? 'GD' : 'GS';
            const teamBadge = getTeamBadge(m.team);
            const statusBadge = getStatusBadge(m.status);

            return `<tr>
                <td class="mono text-xs text-gray-600">${m.no}</td>
                <td>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <div class="w-7 h-7 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center font-bold text-xs flex-shrink-0 ${pillarClass}" style="background:rgba(230,57,70,0.15);">
                            ${m.name[0].toUpperCase()}
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            <p class="text-white font-medium text-sm">${esc(m.name)}</p>
                            ${isRegistered ? '<p class="text-green-400 text-xs">Registered</p>' : '<p class="text-gray-600 text-xs">Not registered</p>'}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </td>
                <td class="mono text-xs text-gray-400">${esc(m.id)}</td>
                <td><span class="badge ${pillarClass}">${pillarShort}</span></td>
                <td class="text-xs text-gray-400">${m.gen}</td>
                <td>${teamBadge}</td>
                <td>${statusBadge}</td>
                <td class="font-bold text-white" style="font-family:'Rajdhani',sans-serif;">${xp}</td>
                <td>
                    <button onclick="viewDetail(${m.no})" class="btn-secondary text-xs py-1 px-2">View</button>
                </td>
            </tr>`;
        }).join('');

        document.getElementById('tableBody').innerHTML = html;
    }

    window.prevPage = () => { if (currentPage > 1) { currentPage--; renderTable(); } };
    window.nextPage = () => {
        if (currentPage * PAGE_SIZE < filteredMembers.length) { currentPage++; renderTable(); }
    };

    // ============================================================
    // Detail modal
    // ============================================================
    window.viewDetail = function(no) {
        const m = allMembers.find(x => x.no === no);
        if (!m) return;
        const fsData = firestoreXPMap[m.id] || {};
        const xp = fsData.xp !== undefined ? fsData.xp : 'Not registered';
        const role = fsData.role || '-';

        document.getElementById('memberDetailContent').innerHTML = `
            <div class="flex items-center gap-4 mb-5">
                <div class="w-14 h-14 rounded-xl bg-red-500/20 border border-red-500/30 flex items-center justify-center text-white font-bold text-2xl">
                    ${m.name[0].toUpperCase()}
                </div>
                <div>
                    <h4 class="text-white font-bold text-lg">${esc(m.name)}</h4>
                    <p class="mono text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">${esc(m.id)}</p>
                    <div class="flex gap-2 mt-1.5">
                        ${getStatusBadge(m.status)}
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 text-sm">
                <div class="bg-white/5 rounded-lg p-3">
                    <p class="text-gray-500 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-1">Pillar</p>
                    <p class="text-white">${m.pillar}</p>
                </div>
                <div class="bg-white/5 rounded-lg p-3">
                    <p class="text-gray-500 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-1">Generation</p>
                    <p class="text-white">${m.gen}</p>
                </div>
                <div class="bg-white/5 rounded-lg p-3">
                    <p class="text-gray-500 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-1">Team</p>
                    ${m.team ? getTeamBadge(m.team) : '<p class="text-gray-500">-</p>'}
                </div>
                <div class="bg-white/5 rounded-lg p-3">
                    <p class="text-gray-500 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-1">System Role</p>
                    <p class="text-white">${role}</p>
                </div>
                <div class="bg-white/5 rounded-lg p-3">
                    <p class="text-gray-500 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-1">Total XP</p>
                    <p class="text-white font-bold text-xl" style="font-family:'Rajdhani',sans-serif;">${xp}</p>
                </div>
                <div class="bg-white/5 rounded-lg p-3">
                    <p class="text-gray-500 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-1">Account</p>
                    <p class="${fsData.registered ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-gray-500'} text-sm">${fsData.registered ? 'Registered' : 'Not registered yet'}</p>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
        document.getElementById('modalDetail').classList.add('show');
    };

    window.closeModal = function() {
        document.getElementById('modalDetail').classList.remove('show');
    };

    // ============================================================
    // Export CSV
    // ============================================================
    window.exportCSV = function() {
        const rows = [['No','Name','ID Player','Pillar','Gen','Team','Status','XP']];
        filteredMembers.forEach(m => {
            const fsData = firestoreXPMap[m.id] || {};
            rows.push([m.no, m.name, m.id, m.pillar, m.gen, m.team || '-', m.status, fsData.xp || 0]);
        });
        const csv = rows.map(r => r.map(c => `"${String(c).replace(/"/g,'""')}"`).join(',')).join('\n');
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([csv], {type:'text/csv'}));
        a.download = `newgame_members_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.csv`;
        a.click();
        showToast('Members exported');
    };

    // ============================================================
    // Logout
    // ============================================================
    window.handleLogout = async function() {
        await signOut(auth);
        window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
    };

    // ============================================================
    // Auto logout 30 menit
    // ============================================================
    let autoLogoutTimer;
    function resetAutoLogout() {
        clearTimeout(autoLogoutTimer);
        autoLogoutTimer = setTimeout(async () => {
            await signOut(auth);
            window.location.href = '/public/pages/login.html';
        }, 30 * 60 * 1000);
    }
    ['click','keypress','scroll','touchstart'].forEach(e => document.addEventListener(e, resetAutoLogout));
    resetAutoLogout();

    // ============================================================
    // Helper functions
    // ============================================================
    function getStatusBadge(s) {
        const map = { ACTIVE:'badge-active', AFK:'badge-afk', NPC:'badge-npc', RESIGN:'badge-resign', GLORY:'badge-glory' };
        return `<span class="badge ${map[s] || 'badge-resign'}">${s||'-'}</span>`;
    }

    function getTeamBadge(t) {
        if (!t || t === '' || t === '?????') return `<span class="text-gray-600 text-xs">-</span>`;
        const map = {
            Core:'team-core', Project:'team-project', Training:'team-training',
            FamilyGame:'team-familygame', Alliance:'team-alliance', Inventory:'team-inventory',
            DesignCraft:'team-designcraft', NewMember:'team-newmember', NPC:'badge-npc'
        };
        return `<span class="badge ${map[t] || ''}">${t}</span>`;
    }

    function esc(s) {
        return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');
    }

    function showToast(msg, type='success') {
        const t = document.createElement('div');
        t.className = `toast toast-${type}`;
        t.innerHTML = `<span>${esc(msg)}</span>`;
        document.getElementById('toastContainer').appendChild(t);
        setTimeout(() => { t.style.opacity='0'; t.style.transition='opacity 0.3s'; setTimeout(()=>t.remove(),300); }, 3500);
    }
</script>
</body>
</html>

// ============================================================
// Navigasi terpusat â€” semua path ada di sini
// Jika ada perubahan path, cukup ubah di file ini saja
// ============================================================

export const PATHS = {
    login:          '/public/pages/login.html',
    dashboard:      '/public/pages/dashboard.html',
    admin:          '/public/pages/admin.html',
    members:        '/public/pages/members.html',
    leaderboard:    '/public/pages/leaderboard.html',
    logs:           '/public/pages/logs.html',
    changePassword: '/public/pages/change-password.html',
    scanQR:         '/index.html',
};

// Redirect helper
export function goTo(page) {
    window.location.href = PATHS[page] || PATHS.dashboard;
}

// Cek role apakah boleh akses halaman admin
export function canAccessAdmin(role) {
    return ['admin', 'inventori', 'superadmin', 'presiden'].includes(role);
}

// Cek role apakah boleh akses import CSV
export function canImportCSV(role) {
    return ['superadmin', 'presiden'].includes(role);
}

// Cek role apakah boleh edit XP
export function canEditXP(role) {
    return ['inventori', 'admin', 'superadmin', 'presiden'].includes(role);
}

// Cek role apakah boleh generate QR dan manage event
export function canManageEvents(role) {
    return ['admin', 'superadmin', 'presiden'].includes(role);
}

<script type="module">
    import { initializeApp, getApps } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js';
    import { getAuth, onAuthStateChanged } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-auth.js';
    import {
        getFirestore, doc, getDoc, setDoc, updateDoc, addDoc,
        collection, Timestamp, writeBatch
    } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-firestore.js';

    const firebaseConfig = {
            apiKey: "AIzaSyD6AqPbmW4UM1d1o8caBWSIi61yQsxxsGk",
            authDomain: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebaseapp.com",
            projectId: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame",
            storageBucket: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebasestorage.app",
            messagingSenderId: "377822320778",
            appId: "1:377822320778:web:f7305bb71019f670ccf573"
    };

    const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
    const auth = getAuth(app);
    const db = getFirestore(app);

    // Ambil token dari URL
    const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const tokenId = params.get('token');

    function show(id) {
        ['stateProcessing','stateSuccess','stateError','stateLogin'].forEach(s => {
            document.getElementById(s).classList.add('hidden');
        });
        document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('hidden');
    }

    if (!tokenId) {
        show('stateError');
        document.getElementById('errorMsg').textContent = 'Invalid QR code â€” no token found';
    } else {
        onAuthStateChanged(auth, async (user) => {
            if (!user || !user.emailVerified) {
                show('stateLogin');
                return;
            }

            try {
                // Generate fingerprint
                const components = [navigator.userAgent, screen.width+'x'+screen.height, navigator.language];
                const str = components.join('|');
                const buffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', new TextEncoder().encode(str));
                const fp = Array.from(new Uint8Array(buffer)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2,'0')).join('');

                const tokenRef = doc(db, 'tokens', tokenId);
                const userRef = doc(db, 'users', user.uid);

                const [tokenSnap, userSnap] = await Promise.all([getDoc(tokenRef), getDoc(userRef)]);

                if (!tokenSnap.exists()) throw new Error('Invalid QR code');
                const token = tokenSnap.data();
                if (token.used) throw new Error('QR code already used');

                const now = new Date();
                const exp = token.expiresAt.toDate ? token.expiresAt.toDate() : new Date(token.expiresAt.seconds * 1000);
                if (now > exp) throw new Error('QR code expired');

                const eventSnap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'events', token.eventId));
                if (!eventSnap.exists() || eventSnap.data().status !== 'active') throw new Error('Event not active');

               if (!userSnap.exists()) {
    throw new Error('Account not found');
}

                const userData = userSnap.data();
                console.log("USER DATA:", userData);

                if (userData.status === 'suspended') {
                throw new Error('Account not active');
}
                const attId = `${token.eventId}_${user.uid}`;
                const attSnap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'attendance', attId));
                if (attSnap.exists()) throw new Error('Already attended');

                const event = eventSnap.data();
                const xp = event.xpReward || 10;
                const total = (userData.xpCache || 0) + xp;

                const batch = writeBatch(db);
                batch.update(tokenRef, { used: true, usedBy: user.uid, usedAt: Timestamp.now(), deviceFingerprint: fp });
                batch.set(doc(db, 'attendance', attId), {
                    eventId: token.eventId, eventName: event.name, userId: user.uid,
                    status: 'present', xpChange: xp, deviceFingerprint: fp, attendedAt: Timestamp.now()
                });
                batch.update(userRef, { xpCache: total, attendanceCount: (userData.attendanceCount || 0) + 1, lastAttendedAt: Timestamp.now() });
                await batch.commit();

                document.getElementById('successEvent').textContent = event.name;
                document.getElementById('successXP').textContent = `+${xp}`;
                show('stateSuccess');

            } catch (err) {
                document.getElementById('errorMsg').textContent = err.message || 'Failed to record attendance';
                show('stateError');
            }
        });
    }
</script>
</body>
</html>

                            <p class="text-white font-semibold text-sm" id="eventNameDisplay">-</p>

                    </div>
                </div>

                <!-- Scanner area -->
                <div class="p-4">
                    <div class="relative mb-4" style="border-radius:12px;overflow:hidden;">
                        <div id="reader" style="width:100%;"></div>
                        <!-- Corner overlays -->
                        <div class="scan-corner tl"></div>

                    <p class="text-gray-400 text-xs text-center">Point your camera at the QR code displayed on screen</p>

                <!-- Manual token input (fallback) -->
                <div class="p-4 pt-0">
                    <details class="text-xs text-gray-600">
                        <summary class="cursor-pointer hover:text-gray-400 transition">Having trouble scanning?</summary>
                        <div class="mt-3 space-y-2">
                            <input type="text" id="manualTokenInput" placeholder="Enter token manually..." style="background:rgba(255,255,255,0.05);color:white;padding:8px 12px;border-radius:8px;border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1);font-size:12px;width:100%;">

                        </div>

            <!-- STATE: Processing -->
            <div class="state-card glass rounded-2xl p-8 text-center" id="stateProcessing">
                <div class="w-12 h-12 border-2 border-red-500 border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin mx-auto mb-4"></div>
                <h2 class="text-xl font-bold text-white mb-2">Processing...</h2>
                <p class="text-gray-400 text-sm">Verifying your attendance</p>
            </div>

            <!-- STATE: Success -->
            <div class="state-card glass rounded-2xl p-8 text-center success-anim" id="stateSuccess">
                <div class="w-20 h-20 rounded-full bg-green-500/20 border-2 border-green-400 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
                    <svg class="w-10 h-10 text-green-400" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="3" d="M5 13l4 4L19 7"/></svg>
                </div>
                <h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-white mb-1" style="font-family:'Rajdhani',sans-serif;">Attendance Recorded!</h2>
                <p class="text-gray-400 text-sm mb-4" id="successEventName">-</p>
                <div class="bg-green-500/10 border border-green-500/30 rounded-xl p-4 mb-4">
                    <p class="text-green-400 text-xs uppercase tracking-wider mb-1">XP Earned</p>
                    <p class="text-4xl font-bold text-green-400" style="font-family:'Rajdhani',sans-serif;" id="successXP">+0</p>
                    <p class="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-1" id="successStreak">-</p>
                </div>
                <div class="text-left space-y-2 mb-6">
                    <div class="flex justify-between text-sm">
                        <span class="text-gray-400">Total XP</span>
                        <span class="text-white font-bold" id="successTotalXP">-</span>

                        <span class="text-gray-400">Current Level</span>

                        <span class="text-gray-400">Streak</span>
                        <span class="text-white font-bold" id="successStreakCount">- days</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <button onclick="resetToScanner()" class="btn-primary w-full justify-center">Done</button>
            </div>

            <!-- STATE: Error -->
            <div class="state-card glass rounded-2xl p-8 text-center error-anim" id="stateError">
                <div class="w-20 h-20 rounded-full bg-red-500/20 border-2 border-red-500 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
                    <svg class="w-10 h-10 text-red-400" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M6 18L18 6M6 6l12 12"/></svg>
                </div>
                <h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-white mb-2" style="font-family:'Rajdhani',sans-serif;">Failed</h2>
                <p class="text-red-400 text-sm mb-6" id="errorMessage">Something went wrong</p>
                <button onclick="resetToScanner()" class="btn-primary w-full justify-center">Try Again</button>
            </div>

            <!-- STATE: Already attended -->
            <div class="state-card glass rounded-2xl p-8 text-center" id="stateAlreadyAttended">

                    <svg class="w-10 h-10 text-blue-400" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M9 12l2 2 4-4m6 2a9 9 0 11-18 0 9 9 0 0118 0z"/></svg>
                </div>
                <h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-white mb-2">Already Recorded</h2>
                <p class="text-blue-400 text-sm mb-4">Your attendance for this event has already been recorded.</p>
                <a href="public/pages/dashboard.html" class="btn-secondary w-full justify-center">Go to Dashboard</a>
            </div>

        </div>
    </div>

<script type="module">
    import { initializeApp, getApps } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js';
    import { getAuth, onAuthStateChanged, signOut } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-auth.js';
    import {
        getFirestore, doc, getDoc, setDoc, updateDoc, addDoc,
        collection, query, where, limit, getDocs, serverTimestamp, Timestamp, writeBatch
    } from 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-firestore.js';

    const firebaseConfig = {
            apiKey: "AIzaSyD6AqPbmW4UM1d1o8caBWSIi61yQsxxsGk",
            authDomain: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebaseapp.com",
            projectId: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame",
            storageBucket: "qr-absensi-unandnewgame.firebasestorage.app",
            messagingSenderId: "377822320778",
            appId: "1:377822320778:web:f7305bb71019f670ccf573"
    };

    const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
    const auth = getAuth(app);
    const db = getFirestore(app);

    let currentUser = null;
    let userData = null;
    let activeEvent = null;
    let scanner = null;
    let isProcessing = false;
    let deviceFingerprint = null;

    // ============================================================
    // Tampilkan satu state, sembunyikan yang lain
    // ============================================================
    function showState(name) {
        document.querySelectorAll('.state-card').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
        const el = document.getElementById(`state${name}`);
        if (el) el.classList.add('active');
    }

    showState('Loading');

    // ============================================================
    // Generate device fingerprint
    // ============================================================
    async function genFingerprint() {
        const components = [
            navigator.userAgent,
            screen.width + 'x' + screen.height,
            Intl.DateTimeFormat().resolvedOptions().timeZone,
            navigator.language,
            navigator.hardwareConcurrency || 0
        ];
        try {
            const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
            const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
            ctx.font = '14px Arial';
            ctx.fillText('NEWGAME-fp', 2, 2);
            components.push(canvas.toDataURL());
        } catch (e) {}
        const str = components.join('|');
        const buffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', new TextEncoder().encode(str));
        return Array.from(new Uint8Array(buffer)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2,'0')).join('');
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Auth check
    // ============================================================
    onAuthStateChanged(auth, async (user) => {
        if (!user || !user.emailVerified) {
            showState('NotLoggedIn');
            return;
        }

        const userDoc = await getDoc(doc(db, 'users', user.uid));
        if (!userDoc.exists() || userDoc.data().status === 'suspended') {
            await signOut(auth);
            showState('NotLoggedIn');
            return;
        }

        currentUser = user;
        userData = userDoc.data();
        deviceFingerprint = await genFingerprint();

        // Render topbar
        document.getElementById('topbarName').textContent = userData.name || user.email;
        document.getElementById('topbarDivision').textContent = userData.division || '-';

        await checkActiveEvent();
        setupAutoLogout();
    });

    // ============================================================
    // Cek event aktif
    // ============================================================
    window.checkActiveEvent = async function() {
        showState('Loading');
        try {
            const q = query(collection(db, 'events'), where('status', '==', 'active'), limit(1));
            const snap = await getDocs(q);

            if (snap.empty) {
                showState('NoEvent');
                return;
            }

            activeEvent = { id: snap.docs[0].id, ...snap.docs[0].data() };
            document.getElementById('eventNameDisplay').textContent = activeEvent.name;
            document.getElementById('eventXPDisplay').textContent = `+${activeEvent.xpReward || 10} XP for attendance`;

            // Cek apakah sudah hadir
            const attId = `${activeEvent.id}_${currentUser.uid}`;
            const attDoc = await getDoc(doc(db, 'attendance', attId));
            if (attDoc.exists()) {
                showState('AlreadyAttended');
                return;
            }

            showState('Scanner');
            startScanner();

        } catch (err) {
            console.error('checkActiveEvent error:', err);
            showState('NoEvent');
        }
    };

    // ============================================================
    // Start QR scanner
    // ============================================================
    function startScanner() {
        if (scanner) { try { scanner.stop(); } catch(e){} }

        scanner = new Html5Qrcode('reader');
        scanner.start(
            { facingMode: 'environment' },
            { fps: 10, qrbox: { width: 250, height: 250 } },
            (decodedText) => {
                if (isProcessing) return;
                processQR(decodedText);
            },
            (err) => {}
        ).catch(err => {
            console.error('Camera error:', err);
        });
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Proses QR yang di-scan
    // ============================================================
    async function processQR(text) {
        if (isProcessing) return;
        isProcessing = true;

        // Stop scanner segera
        try { if (scanner) scanner.stop(); } catch(e){}

        showState('Processing');

        try {
            // Extract token dari URL atau langsung token ID
            let tokenId = text;
            if (text.includes('token=')) {
                const url = new URL(text);
                tokenId = url.searchParams.get('token');
            }

            if (!tokenId) throw new Error('Invalid QR code format');

            await processAttendance(tokenId);

        } catch (err) {
            console.error('processQR error:', err);
            showError(err.message || 'Invalid QR code');
        }
    }

    window.processManualToken = function() {
        const token = document.getElementById('manualTokenInput').value.trim();
        if (!token) return;
        processQR(token);
    };

    // ============================================================
    // Validasi dan proses absensi â€” semua di client
    // Logika sama seperti yang ada di Cloud Functions
    // ============================================================
    async function processAttendance(tokenId) {
        try {
            const tokenRef = doc(db, 'tokens', tokenId);
            const userRef = doc(db, 'users', currentUser.uid);

            const [tokenSnap, userSnap] = await Promise.all([
                getDoc(tokenRef),
                getDoc(userRef)
            ]);

            // Validasi token
            if (!tokenSnap.exists()) throw new Error('Invalid QR code');
            const token = tokenSnap.data();
            if (token.used) throw new Error('QR code already used â€” wait for next refresh');

            // Validasi expiry menggunakan timestamp dari server
            const now = new Date();
            const expiresAt = token.expiresAt.toDate ? token.expiresAt.toDate() : new Date(token.expiresAt.seconds * 1000);
            if (now > expiresAt) throw new Error('QR code has expired â€” wait for next refresh');

            // Validasi event masih aktif
            const eventSnap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'events', token.eventId));
            if (!eventSnap.exists() || eventSnap.data().status !== 'active') {
                throw new Error('Event is no longer active');
            }

            // Validasi user
            if (!userSnap.exists()) throw new Error('Account not found');
            const user = userSnap.data();
            if (user.status === 'suspended') throw new Error('Your account has been suspended');

            // Cek double attend
            const attId = `${token.eventId}_${currentUser.uid}`;
            const attSnap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'attendance', attId));
            if (attSnap.exists()) {
                showState('AlreadyAttended');
                isProcessing = false;
                return;
            }

            // Hitung XP dan streak
            const event = eventSnap.data();
            const xpReward = event.xpReward || 10;
            const currentXP = user.xpCache || 0;
            const currentStreak = user.streak || 0;
            let newStreak = 1;
            let streakBonus = 0;

            if (user.lastAttendedAt) {
                const lastDate = user.lastAttendedAt.toDate ? user.lastAttendedAt.toDate() : new Date(user.lastAttendedAt.seconds * 1000);
                const diffDays = Math.floor((now - lastDate) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
                if (diffDays <= 7) {
                    newStreak = currentStreak + 1;
                    if (newStreak % 5 === 0) streakBonus = 5;
                }
            }

            const totalXP = currentXP + xpReward + streakBonus;
            const level = Math.floor(totalXP / 100) + 1;

            // Tulis semua data sekaligus
            const batch = writeBatch(db);

            // Mark token as used
            batch.update(tokenRef, {
                used: true,
                usedBy: currentUser.uid,
                usedAt: Timestamp.now(),
                deviceFingerprint
            });

            // Buat attendance record
            batch.set(doc(db, 'attendance', attId), {
                eventId: token.eventId,
                eventName: event.name,
                userId: currentUser.uid,
                status: 'present',
                xpChange: xpReward + streakBonus,
                streakBonus,
                deviceFingerprint,
                attendedAt: Timestamp.now()
            });

            // Update user XP dan streak
            batch.update(userRef, {
                xpCache: totalXP,
                attendanceCount: (user.attendanceCount || 0) + 1,
                streak: newStreak,
                lastAttendedAt: Timestamp.now()
            });

            // XP history
            const xpHistRef = doc(collection(db, 'xpHistory'));
            batch.set(xpHistRef, {
                userId: currentUser.uid,
                eventId: token.eventId,
                change: xpReward + streakBonus,
                reason: `Attended: ${event.name}`,
                type: 'attendance',
                timestamp: Timestamp.now()
            });

            await batch.commit();

            // Log
            await addDoc(collection(db, 'logs'), {
                userId: currentUser.uid,
                action: 'attend',
                result: 'success',
                eventId: token.eventId,
                eventName: event.name,
                deviceFingerprint,
                timestamp: Timestamp.now()
            });

            // Tampilkan sukses
            showSuccessState({
                xpGained: xpReward + streakBonus,
                streakBonus,
                newStreak,
                totalXP,
                level,
                eventName: event.name
            });

        } catch (err) {
            console.error('processAttendance error:', err);
            showError(err.message);
        }
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Tampilkan state sukses
    // ============================================================
    function showSuccessState(result) {
        document.getElementById('successEventName').textContent = result.eventName;
        document.getElementById('successXP').textContent = `+${result.xpGained}`;
        document.getElementById('successTotalXP').textContent = `${result.totalXP} XP`;
        document.getElementById('successLevel').textContent = `Level ${result.level}`;
        document.getElementById('successStreakCount').textContent = `${result.newStreak} day${result.newStreak !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
        document.getElementById('successStreak').textContent =
            result.streakBonus > 0 ? `Streak bonus: +${result.streakBonus} XP` : `Streak: ${result.newStreak} days`;

        showState('Success');
        isProcessing = false;

        // XP float animation
        spawnXPFloat(`+${result.xpGained} XP`);
    }

    function showError(msg) {
        document.getElementById('errorMessage').textContent = msg;
        showState('Error');
        isProcessing = false;
    }

    function spawnXPFloat(text) {
        const el = document.createElement('div');
        el.className = 'xp-float';
        el.textContent = text;
        el.style.cssText = `top:40%;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);`;
        document.getElementById('xpFloatContainer').appendChild(el);
        setTimeout(() => el.remove(), 2000);
    }

    window.resetToScanner = async function() {
        isProcessing = false;
        await checkActiveEvent();
    };

    // ============================================================
    // Auto logout 30 menit
    // ============================================================
    function setupAutoLogout() {
        let t;
        const r = () => {
            clearTimeout(t);
            t = setTimeout(async () => {
                try { if (scanner) scanner.stop(); } catch(e){}
                await signOut(auth);
                window.location.href = 'public/pages/login.html';
            }, 30 * 60 * 1000);
        };
        ['click','keypress','scroll','touchstart'].forEach(e => document.addEventListener(e, r));
        r();
    }
</script>
</body>
</html>
